### [34] [AgentFinVQA: A Deployable Multi-Agent Pipeline for Auditable Financial Chart QA](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19782v1)
*Aravind Narayanan,Shaina Raza*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 多agent pipeline用于图表QA，含规划、验证，方法可迁移

TL;DR: 提出AgentFinVQA，一种可审计、本地部署的多智能体金融图表问答系统，在FinMME上分别提升专有和开放权重基线7.68和4.84个百分点，验证者提供有效置信信号，错误分析指明改进方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受监管的金融图表问答需要可信任和本地部署，现有系统不透明且依赖专有API，缺乏结合可审计性与本地部署的方案。

Method: 多智能体流水线，将查询分解为规划、OCR、图例理解、视觉检查和验证，每一步记录在可追踪的模型评估包（MEP）中。

Result: 在FinMME上，使用专有骨干（Gemini-3 Flash）提升7.68个百分点（71.24% vs 63.56%），使用开放权重（Qwen3.6-27B-FP8）提升4.84个百分点；验证者置信信号有效（确认答案68.2% vs 修订答案55.6%）；错误分析表明问题误解、图例混淆和提取错误占失败的三分之二，且验证者最难检测。

Conclusion: 可审计的本地部署金融图表QA是可行的，开放权重系统在保持大部分准确性提升的同时实现了完全数据驻留。

中文摘要：在受监管环境中的金融图表问答需要的不止是准确性：从业者在依赖答案之前必须知道哪些答案可以信任，而且许多机构无法将客户数据发送给外部模型提供商。然而，现有的图表问答代理注重准确性且不透明，大多数假设专有API访问；据我们所知，没有一个代理能在不显著降低准确性的情况下将可审计性与本地部署能力结合起来。我们提出了AgentFinVQA，这是一个多智能体流水线，它将每个查询分解为规划、OCR、图例理解、视觉检查和验证，并在每个样本的可追踪模型评估包（MEP）中记录每一步。在FinMME上，AgentFinVQA在使用专有骨干（Gemini-3 Flash）时比主骨干匹配的零样本基线提高了+7.68个百分点（71.24% vs. 63.56%，McNemar p ≈ 1.1×10^{-16}），在使用本地服务的开放权重Qwen3.6-27B-FP8时提高了+4.84个百分点。验证者的判断也作为有用的置信度信号（确认答案与修订答案的精确准确率分别为68.2% vs. 55.6%），支持人在环审核路由。错误分析表明，问题误解、图例混淆和提取错误占了几乎三分之二的失败，并且是验证者最难检测的类别，这为未来工作指明了明确的方向。这些结果共同表明，可审计的本地部署金融图表QA是可行的，并且开放权重系统在保持大部分准确性提升的同时实现了完全数据驻留。我们发布代码以支持可重复评估。

Original abstract: Financial chart question answering in regulated settings demands more than accuracy: practitioners must know which answers to trust before acting on them, and many institutions cannot send client data to external model providers. Yet existing chart-QA agents are accuracy-focused and opaque, and most assume proprietary API access; to our knowledge, none combines auditability with on-premise deployability without significant accuracy compromise. We present AgentFinVQA, a multi-agent pipeline that decomposes each query into planning, OCR, legend grounding, visual inspection, and verification, recording every step in a traceable Model Evaluation Packet (MEP) per sample. On FinMME, AgentFinVQA improves $+7.68$ pp over a primary-backbone matched zero-shot baseline with a proprietary backbone (Gemini-3 Flash; 71.24% vs. 63.56%, McNemar $p \approx 1.1 \times 10^{-16}$), and $+4.84$ pp with open-weights Qwen3.6-27B-FP8 served locally. The verifier's verdict also serves as a useful confidence signal (68.2% vs. 55.6% exact accuracy on confirmed vs. revised answers), enabling human-in-the-loop review routing. Error analysis shows that question misunderstanding, legend confusion and extraction error account for nearly two-thirds of failures and are the categories least detected by the verifier, identifying clear directions for future work. Together these results show that auditable, on-premise financial chart QA is practical and that the open-weights system keeps most of the accuracy gains while enabling full data residency. We release our code to support reproducible evaluation.

</details>


### [35] [ORAgentBench: Can LLM Agents Solve Challenging Operations Research Tasks End to End?](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19787v1)
*Jiajun Li,Mingshu Cai,Yixuan Li,Yu Ding,Ran Hou,Guanyu Nie,Xiongwei Han,Wanyuan Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 端到端运筹学agent benchmark，直接相关agent评估

TL;DR: 提出的ORAgentBench基准评估了大模型在端到端运筹学任务中的表现，发现当前智能体远未达到可靠水平，最佳智能体仅通过35.51%的任务，错误主要由战略弱点导致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有OR评估通常解耦建模与求解，依赖预形式化实例，缺乏对完整工作流的测试，因此需要更真实的基准来评估LLM代理的OR能力。

Method: 构建了包含107个任务的可执行基准ORAgentBench，每个任务包含隔离环境、自然语言简介、多文件数据、配置工件和提交模式，通过隐藏验证器评估模式有效性、硬约束可行性和目标质量，并使用14种前沿智能体配置进行实验。

Result: 最佳智能体通过35.51%的所有任务和20.59%的困难任务，许多可行提交质量低于阈值；失败主要由战略弱点导致，OR特定过程技能仅提高可行性而非质量。

Conclusion: OR智能体的进步需要超越生成合理优化代码，转向可靠、高质量的操作决策。

中文摘要：大型语言模型越来越多地被部署为可执行环境中多步骤任务的自主智能体，但它们在现实运筹学（OR）工作中的能力仍不清楚。现有的OR评估通常将建模与求解解耦，依赖于预形式化或纯文本实例，很少测试从操作工件到验证决策的完整流程。在这项工作中，我们引入了ORAgentBench，一个基于执行的可信基准，用于评估自主智能体在具有挑战性的端到端运筹学任务上的表现。它包含107个经过人工审查的任务，涵盖多样化的运行场景，每个任务都封装在一个隔离的环境中，包含自然语言简介、多文件数据、配置工件以及所需的提交模式。智能体必须编写并运行解决方案代码，其提交由隐藏验证器评估模式有效性、硬约束可行性和归一化目标质量。使用14种前沿智能体模型的实验表明，当前智能体远未达到可靠的OR实践。最佳智能体仅通过35.51%的所有任务和20.59%的困难任务，许多可行提交仍低于所需的质量阈值。失败分析进一步表明，错误主要由战略弱点主导，包括遗漏操作规则、脆弱的公式化、弱的可行解构建以及不充分的解改进。OR特定的过程技能提高了困难任务的可行性，但不能可靠地提高解质量或通过率。这些结果表明，OR智能体的进步需要超越合理的优化代码，转向可靠、高质量的操作决策。

Original abstract: Large language models are increasingly deployed as autonomous agents for multi-step tasks in executable environments, yet their ability to perform realistic operations research (OR) work remains unclear. Existing OR evaluations often decouple modeling from solving, rely on pre-formalized or text-only instances, and rarely test the full workflow from operational artifacts to validated decisions. In this work, we introduce ORAgentBench, an execution-grounded benchmark for evaluating autonomous agents on challenging end-to-end operations research tasks. It contains 107 human-reviewed tasks across diverse operational scenarios, each packaged in an isolated environment with a natural-language brief, multi-file data, configuration artifacts, and a required submission schema. Agents must write and run solution code, and their submissions are evaluated by hidden validators for schema validity, hard-constraint feasibility, and normalized objective quality. Experiments with fourteen frontier agent-model configurations show that current agents remain far from reliable OR practice. The best agent passes only 35.51% of all tasks and 20.59% of hard tasks, and many feasible submissions still fall below the required quality threshold. Failure analysis further shows that errors are dominated by strategic weaknesses, including missed operational rules, brittle formulations, weak feasible-solution construction, and insufficient solution improvement. OR-specific procedural skills increase hard-task feasibility, but do not reliably improve solution quality or pass rate. These results suggest that progress in OR agents requires moving beyond plausible optimization code toward dependable, high-quality operational decision-making.

</details>


### [36] [Think Again or Think Longer? Selective Verification for Budget-Aware Reasoning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19808v1)
*Sajib Acharjee Dip,Dawei Zhou,Liqing Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 选择性验证框架，预算感知推理，通用agent部署策略

TL;DR: 提出选择性验证（SEVRA）作为服务层控制器，在保持准确率的同时减少推理成本和有害翻转，但更优策略通常是先调大初始解算预算。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 测试时额外推理并非均匀有益，可能浪费计算或引入错误，因此需要高效分配验证资源。

Method: 提出SEVRA，一个服务层控制器，基于服务可见的尝试状态训练可恢复性感知门，决定是保留冻结求解器的初始答案还是调用主动验证。

Result: 在MATH-500上，SEVRA达到76.3%准确率（始终验证75.5%），减少后生成令牌26.8%，有害翻转从2.2%降至1.0%；但更长初始解算（8192令牌）以更低总令牌达到76.0%。在GSM上仅验证3.0%示例，准确率提升1.1%，验证令牌减少91.2%；CommonsenseQA上始终验证有害，Self-Consistency@5提升准确率但成本高。

Conclusion: 部署规则：先调整初始解算预算，再在需要明确检查、有限重试、可审计性或回归风险控制时使用选择性恢复。

中文摘要：测试时推理越来越多地被用作服务时的控制旋钮，但额外的推理并非均匀有价值：它可能修复失败的尝试，在已正确的答案上浪费计算，或引入有害的答案变化。我们将其作为一个部署分配问题而非新验证器问题来研究。我们引入了\sevra，选择性验证用于推理分配，一个服务层控制器，决定是保留冻结求解器的初始答案还是调用主动验证。使用冻结的Qwen3-4B求解器，我们记录干预结果并从服务可见的尝试状态训练可恢复性感知门。在\mathfive上，选择性验证达到了76.3%的准确率，而始终验证为75.5%，同时将生成后令牌减少了26.8%，有害翻转从2.2%降至1.0%。然而，一个8,192令牌的初始求解达到76.0%的准确率，总模型令牌减少28%，表明选择性恢复有用但并非测试的最佳成本前沿。在冻结迁移到\gsm时，选择性策略仅验证3.0%的示例，准确率从93.4%提高到94.5%，相对于始终验证减少了91.2%的验证令牌；同样，更长的初始求解以更少的实际令牌达到相同准确率。在CommonsenseQA上，始终开启的验证有害，而Self-Consistency@5以约五倍的实际令牌成本提高了准确率。最终部署规则是：首先调整初始预算，然后在明确检查、有限重试、可审计性或回归风险控制重要时使用选择性恢复。

Original abstract: Test-time reasoning is increasingly used as a serving-time control knob, but extra reasoning is not uniformly valuable: it can repair failed attempts, waste compute on already-correct answers, or introduce harmful answer changes. We study this as a deployment allocation problem rather than a new-verifier problem. We introduce \sevra, Selective Verification for Reasoning Allocation, a serving-layer controller that decides whether to preserve a frozen solver's initial answer or invoke active verification. Using a frozen Qwen3-4B solver, we log intervention outcomes and train recoverability-aware gates from serving-visible attempt state. On \mathfive, selective verification reaches 76.3\% accuracy, compared with 75.5\% for always verifying, while reducing post-generation tokens by 26.8\% and harmful flips from 2.2\% to 1.0\%. However, an 8,192-token initial solve reaches 76.0\% accuracy with 28\% fewer total model tokens, showing that selective recovery is useful but not the best tested cost frontier. In frozen transfer to \gsm, the selective policy verifies only 3.0\% of examples, improves accuracy from 93.4\% to 94.5\%, and reduces verification tokens by 91.2\% relative to always verifying; again, a longer initial solve matches its accuracy with fewer realized tokens. On CommonsenseQA, always-on verification hurts, while Self-Consistency@5 improves accuracy at about five times the realized token cost. The resulting deployment rule is: tune the initial budget first, then use selective recovery when explicit checks, bounded retries, auditability, or regression-risk control matter.

### [37] [Human-on-the-Loop Orchestration for AI-Assisted Legal Discovery](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19812v1)
*Anushree Sinha,Srivaths Ranganathan,Abhishek Dharmaratnakar,Debanshu Das*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: HOTL编排架构，多agent工作流，可迁移至其他agent系统

TL;DR: 提出轨迹崩溃故障分类、四层验证架构和HOTL阈值，将特权放弃风险降低61%且仅需律师审查少于25%文档。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自主LLM代理在电子发现中因多步推理链的复合错误可能构成法律失职，现有方法缺乏对轨迹崩溃等特定故障的防护。

Method: 提出结构化故障分类、四层验证架构（规划、推理、执行、不确定性量化），并在合成语料库上模拟HOTL升级阈值。

中文摘要：自主大型语言模型（LLM）代理越来越多地应用于电子发现（e-discovery），在此背景下，多步推理链中的复合错误可能构成法律失职。与单轮检索不同，在特权文档语料库上运行的代理工作流表现出一种我们称之为“轨迹崩溃”的故障：早期错误分类悄然传播，导致整个特权审查无效。本文做出三项贡献。首先，我们提出一个按功能阶段组织的法律信息检索中代理故障的结构化分类。其次，我们引入一个四层验证架构——涵盖规划、推理、执行和不确定性量化——旨在防止这些故障复合。第三，我们展示了一项在合成电子发现语料库上的初步模拟研究，该研究证明了强制性人在回路（HOTL）升级阈值相对于完全自主基线如何降低特权放弃风险。我们的结果表明，与完全自主部署相比，校准的不确定性阈值可以将特权放弃风险降低高达61%，同时将不到四分之一的文档路由至律师审查。

Original abstract: Autonomous Large Language Model (LLM) agents are increasingly deployed in electronic discovery (e-discovery), where compounding errors across multi-step reasoning chains can constitute legal malpractice. Unlike single-turn retrieval, agentic workflows operating over privileged document corpora exhibit a class of failure we term "trajectory collapse": an early misclassification silently propagates, rendering an entire privilege review invalid. This paper makes three contributions. First, we propose a structured taxonomy of agentic failures in legal information retrieval, organized by functional stage. Second, we introduce a four-layer verification architecture -- spanning planning, reasoning, execution, and uncertainty quantification -- designed to intercept these failures before they compound. Third, we present a preliminary simulation study on a synthetic e-discovery corpus that demonstrates how mandatory Human-on-the-Loop (HOTL) escalation thresholds reduce privilege-waiver risk relative to fully autonomous baselines. Our results suggest that calibrated uncertainty thresholds can reduce privilege-waiver risk by up to 61% versus fully autonomous deployment, while routing fewer than one quarter of documents to attorney review.

Original abstract: Key Performance Measurement (KPM) forecasting is essential for proactive network management of 5G and next-generation telecom networks. However, existing machine learning (ML) approaches face significant limitations in scalability and explainability, restricting their effectiveness in real-world deployments. We propose TelcoAgent, a foundation model-based framework that enables accurate, scalable, and explainable forecasting of multiple KPMs across diverse network cells without the need for site-specific training. Specifically, the framework comprises three key components: (i) an automated three-agent pipeline that constructs a 3rd Generation Partnership Project (3GPP) knowledge graph directly from specification documents, (ii) a scalable, time-series foundation model (TSFM)-based prediction pipeline to deliver accurate, zero-shot forecasting, and finally (iii) a reasoning and explanation pipeline that provides actionable, domain-grounded diagnostics. Evaluated using a 3-month, real-world, city-scale 5G KPM dataset from a U.S.-based network operator, TelcoAgent demonstrates high forecasting accuracy for all 7 considered KPMs per cell across 200 cells, while delivering explainable insights and actionable instructions to address network degradations.

### [39] [A Systematic Evaluation of Black-Box Uncertainty Estimation Methods for Large Language Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19868v1)
*Jiayi Wang,Xu-Yao Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 黑盒不确定性估计方法系统评估，包含多agent方法，涉及agent可靠性

TL;DR: 对黑盒不确定性估计方法进行系统综述和基准测试，发现无单一方法普遍最优，但基于答案空间推理和混合方法表现较好。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有关于LLMs黑盒UE的研究方法零散，缺乏统一的实证比较。

Method: 系统综述将方法分为五类，构建统一评估框架，在4个模型和4个数据集上基准测试24种方法。

Result: 没有单一方法在所有设置中占优，但答案空间推理和混合方法表现有效。

Conclusion: 发布基准数据和评估框架，为未来研究提供实用指导。

中文摘要：尽管大语言模型（LLMs）在广泛任务中表现出强大能力，但其输出通常不可靠且可能包含幻觉，因此不确定性估计（UE）对于构建可信的LLMs至关重要。实践中，许多主流LLMs只能通过受限API访问，此时logits和隐藏状态等内部信号不可用，使得黑盒UE尤为重要。然而，现有关于LLMs黑盒UE的研究在方法上仍然零散，缺乏统一的实证比较。为填补这一空白，我们系统性地综述了黑盒UE方法，将其分为五类：基于言语化、基于采样、基于解释、多智能体和混合方法。我们进一步构建了统一评估框架，并在4个模型和4个数据集设置上对24种代表性方法进行基准测试。结果表明，没有一种方法在所有设置中始终占优。然而，在答案空间中进行推理和比较候选的方法通常有效，结合多种不确定性信号的混合方法在大多数条件下表现良好。通过发布基准数据和统一评估框架，我们旨在促进可重复比较并支持未来研究，同时我们的实证发现为未来开发LLMs黑盒UE方法提供了实用指导。

Original abstract: Although large language models (LLMs) have shown strong capabilities across a wide range of tasks, their outputs often remain unreliable and may contain hallucinations, making uncertainty estimation (UE) essential for building trustworthy LLMs. In practice, many mainstream LLMs are only accessible through restricted APIs, where internal signals such as logits and hidden states are unavailable, making black-box UE especially important. However, existing work on black-box UE for LLMs remains fragmented in methodology and lacks a unified empirical comparison. To address this gap, we present a systematic review of black-box UE methods and organize them into five categories: verbalization-based, sampling-based, explanation-based, multi-agent, and hybrid methods. We further build a unified evaluation framework and benchmark 24 representative methods across 4 models and 4 dataset settings. Our results show that no single method consistently dominates across all settings. Nevertheless, methods that reason over and compare candidates in the answer space are generally effective, and hybrid methods that combine multiple uncertainty signals perform well under most conditions. By releasing the benchmark data and a unified evaluation framework, we aim to facilitate reproducible comparisons and support future research, while our empirical findings provide practical guidance for developing future black-box UE methods for LLMs.

### [40] [MetaResearcher: Scaling Deep Research via Self-Reflective Reinforcement Learning in Adversarial Virtual Environments](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19893v1)
*Wei Yu,Suxing Liu,Minjie Yu,Jiahao Wang,Zhijian Zheng,Haocheng Deng,Bing Li*

  <summary>Details</summary>

中文摘要：深度研究智能体在自主信息收集与综合方面展现了卓越的能力，但其训练仍受限于模拟环境的静态特性、仅限事实检索的任务设计限制以及基于结果的强化学习效率低下的问题。在这项工作中，我们提出了MetaResearcher，一个新颖的框架，它在四个协同维度上扩展深度研究智能体的训练。首先，我们引入了一个演化虚拟世界，将时间动态和对抗性错误信息注入训练环境，迫使智能体发展来源可信度评估和时间冲突解决能力。其次，我们设计了面向发现的任务——包括假设生成和矛盾解决——超越了简单的事实检索，推动智能体走向真正的研究行为。第三，我们在GRPO框架内提出了一种自我反思的元奖励机制，共同优化答案正确性、搜索路径效率、反思深度和工具调用多样性，直接解决了先前工作中观察到的重复动作循环问题。第四，我们引入了一种异构多智能体群架构，包括专门的侦察兵、过滤器和综合器模型，通过协调的强化学习学习协作研究策略。基于LiteResearcher基础设施，MetaResearcher在训练中需要零边际API成本，同时目标是在基准性能（GAIA、Xbench-DS）和对抗条件下的认知鲁棒性上取得显著改进。我们提出了完整的框架设计、训练方法和计划的实验验证。

Original abstract: Deep research agents have demonstrated remarkable capabilities in autonomous information gathering and synthesis, yet their training remains constrained by the static nature of simulated environments, the limits of fact-retrieval-only task designs, and the inefficiency of outcome-based reinforcement learning. In this work, we propose MetaResearcher, a novel framework that scales deep research agent training across four synergistic dimensions. First, we introduce an Evolving Virtual World that injects temporal dynamics and adversarial misinformation into the training environment, forcing agents to develop source credibility assessment and temporal conflict resolution skills. Second, we design Discovery-Oriented Tasks -- including hypothesis generation and contradiction resolution -- that transcend simple fact retrieval and push agents toward genuine research behaviors. Third, we propose a Self-Reflective Meta-Reward mechanism within the GRPO framework that jointly optimizes for answer correctness, search path efficiency, reflection depth, and tool call diversity, directly addressing the repetitive action loop problem observed in prior work. Fourth, we introduce a Heterogeneous Multi-Agent Swarm architecture comprising specialized Scout, Filter, and Synthesizer models that learn collaborative research strategies through coordinated reinforcement learning. Built upon the LiteResearcher infrastructure, MetaResearcher requires zero marginal API cost for training while targeting substantial improvements in both benchmark performance (GAIA, Xbench-DS) and epistemic robustness under adversarial conditions. We present the complete framework design, training methodology, and planned experimental validation.

### [41] [Multi-Agent Transactive Memory](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19911v1)
*To Eun Kim,Xuhong He,Dishank Jain,Ambuj Agrawal,Negar Arabzadeh,Fernando Diaz*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出多代理可转移记忆（MATM）框架，包含共享轨迹库，生产代理贡献轨迹，消费代理检索轨迹以辅助任务执行。

Result: 在ALFWorld和WebArena环境中的实验表明，MATM改善了下游任务性能并减少了交互步骤，且无需代理间协调或联合训练。

Conclusion: MATM可作为开放代理生态系统中群体级别经验共享的设计模式。

中文摘要：不同能力的LLM代理在多样任务中的分散部署激励了异构代理群体间知识共享的基础设施。正如搜索引擎索引人类生成的工件以支持人类问题解决一样，检索系统可以组织代理生成的工件以供代理群体重用。我们将检索增强生成（它证明了人类创作的工件对单个代理的价值）扩展到支持代理群体的代理生成工件的检索。特别是，代理轨迹编码了可重用的程序性知识，然而这些工件通常在使用一次后被丢弃，或者仅由生成代理保留，迫使新实例化的代理反复重新发现现有解决方案。我们提出了多代理可转移记忆（MATM），这是一个用于群体级别存储和检索代理生成轨迹的框架，其中生产代理将轨迹贡献到共享存储库，消费代理检索它们以改进任务执行。我们关注交互环境（ALFWorld和WebArena），在这些环境中轨迹很长且编码了特别丰富的程序性结构。我们的实验表明，从MATM检索轨迹可以改善下游任务性能并减少交互步骤，而无需协调或联合训练。这些结果将MATM定位为开放代理生态系统中群体级别经验共享的设计模式。

Original abstract: The decentralized deployment of LLM agents with diverse capabilities across diverse tasks motivates infrastructure for knowledge sharing across heterogeneous agent populations. Just as search engines index human-generated artifacts to support human problem solving, retrieval systems can organize agent-generated artifacts for reuse across agent populations. We extend retrieval-augmented generation - which demonstrates the value of human-authored artifacts to individual agents - to retrieval of agent-generated artifacts supporting a population of agents. In particular, agent trajectories encode reusable procedural knowledge, yet these artifacts are typically discarded after a single use or retained only by the producing agent, forcing newly instantiated agents to repeatedly rediscover existing solutions. We propose Multi-Agent Transactive Memory (MATM), a framework for population-level storage and retrieval of agent-generated trajectories, where producer agents contribute trajectories to a shared repository and consumer agents retrieve them to improve task execution. We focus on interactive environments (ALFWorld and WebArena), where trajectories are long and encode especially rich procedural structure. Our experiments demonstrate that retrieving trajectories from MATM improves downstream task performance and reduces interaction steps without coordination or joint training. These results position MATM as a design pattern for population-level experience sharing in open agent ecosystems.

</details>


### [42] [The Tao of Agency: Autotelic AI, Embedded Agency and Dissolution of the Self](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19924v1)

中文摘要：大多数人工智能系统建立在这样的假设上：目标是外生的，由设计者指定。探索当智能体开始生成自己的目标时会发生什么，开启了自生目标AI领域。智能体不仅被期望追求目标，还要发现目标。在本文中，我们通过内在动机、资源驱动先验、因果-干预学习、稳态和嵌入性来追溯其后果；其中嵌入性被发现是自生目标动因的必要但不充分条件。嵌入性以揭示个体化非唯一为代价将智能体个体化，使得相同的动力学承认许多有效的划分，每种划分定义了一个不同的候选自我。因此，自生目标AI最深层次的问题不在于智能体如何生成目标，而在于它如何生成并相对化目标所归属的自我。智能体必须相信自己的边界才能行动，并看穿该边界才能理解。我们将这些发展整合到一个单一框架中，并沿着三个方向扩展：量子公式化，其中智能体-环境切割成为物理的；基于非二元沉思传统的哲学解读；以及一个具体的基于LLM的智能体实例化。

Original abstract: Most artificial intelligence systems are built on the assumption that goals are exogenous and specified by the designer. Exploring what happens when an agent begins generating its own goals opens the field of autotelic AI. Agents are expected not merely to pursue objectives but to discover them. In this article, we trace its consequences through intrinsic motivation, resource-driven priors, causal-interventional learning, homeostasis, and embeddedness; the last of which is found to be a necessary but not sufficient condition for autotelic agency. Embeddedness individuates the agent at the cost of revealing that the individuation is non-unique, such that the same dynamics admit many valid partitions, each defining a different candidate self.
  The deepest problem with autotelic AI is therefore not how the agent generates goals, but how it generates and relativizes the self to which the goals are assigned. The agent must believe in its own boundary in order to act, and see through that boundary in order to understand. We consolidate these developments into a single framework and extend it along three directions: a quantum formulation in which the agent-environment cut becomes physical, a philosophical reading against non-dual contemplative traditions, and a concrete LLM-based agentic instantiation.

### [43] [Advancing DialNav through Automatic Embodied Dialog Augmentation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19948v1)

Original abstract: For embodied agents capable of physical interaction, the capability to create and understand dialog is crucial to ensure both safety and effectiveness. While DialNav~\cite{han2025dialnav} provides a framework for holistic evaluation of the dialog--execution loop in photorealistic indoor navigation, its performance remains limited by a critical scarcity of training data (2K episodes). To address this, we propose an automatic generation pipeline, and construct the \textbf{RAINbow} dataset, a large-scale training dataset with 238K episodes for DialNav. Our pipeline converts existing VLN datasets into multi-turn dialog and creates cost-efficient and high-quality dataset. Then, we introduce two additional complementary advances to unlock the data's full potential: (1) Dual-Strategy Training, a navigation training scheme to align the navigation training with the dynamic dialog-navigation loop, and (2) a localization model that leverages VLN knowledge. By combining these complementary solutions, our model substantially outperforms the baseline in success rate on both \textbf{Val Seen} (58.24, \textbf{+89\%}) and \textbf{Val Unseen} (29.05, \textbf{+100\%}) splits, establishing a new state of the art.

### [44] [ENPIRE: Agentic Robot Policy Self-Improvement in the Real World](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19980v1)
*Wenli Xiao,Jia Xie,Tonghe Zhang,Haotian Lin,Letian "Max" Fu,Haoru Xue,Jalen Lu,Yi Yang,Cunxi Dai,Zi Wang,Jimmy Wu,Guanzhi Wang,S. Shankar Sastry,Ken Goldberg,Linxi "Jim" Fan,Yuke Zhu,Guanya Shi*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出ENPIRE闭环框架，agent自动改进机器人策略，可迁移至代码优化agent。

TL;DR: ENPIRE是一个为编码智能体设计的框架，通过自动重置、验证和策略改进的闭环反馈，使智能体能自主训练灵巧操作策略，在多个任务上达到99%成功率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有机器人操作依赖大量人工监督，编码智能体在数字环境中成功但难以应用于现实，因为缺乏可重复的物理反馈循环。

Method: 提出ENPIRE框架，包含环境模块（EN）、策略改进模块（PI）、评估模块（R）和进化模块（E），形成闭环优化系统。

Result: 在灵巧操作任务（如整理针盒、紧固扎带和工具使用）上，编码智能体自主训练达到99%成功率，且通过机器人集群加速。

Conclusion: ENPIRE展示了编码智能体自主推进现实世界机器人技术的可行性和可扩展性。

中文摘要：实现现实世界中的灵巧机器人操作严重依赖人类监督和算法工程，这成为追求通用物理智能的核心瓶颈。尽管新兴的编码智能体能够生成代码来自动化算法搜索，但它们的成功在很大程度上仍局限于数字环境。我们猜测，自动化机器人研究所缺失的抽象是一个可重复的现实世界策略改进反馈循环：重置场景、执行策略、验证结果并完善下一次迭代。为了弥补这一差距，我们引入了ENPIRE，一个为编码智能体设计的框架，该框架实例化了这一物理反馈例程，包含四个核心模块：环境模块（EN）用于自动重置和验证，策略改进模块（PI）启动策略优化，评估模块（R）用于用一个或多个并行运行的物理机器人评估策略，以及进化模块（E），其中编码智能体分析日志、查阅文献、改进训练基础设施和算法代码以解决失败模式。这个闭环系统将现实世界操作学习转化为可控的优化过程，最大限度地减少人工努力，同时允许在训练方案和智能体变体之间进行公平的消融。在ENPIRE的驱动下，前沿编码智能体可以自主训练策略，在具有挑战性的灵巧操作任务（如整理针盒、紧固扎带和工具使用）上实现99%的成功率，当我们在一个机器人集群中部署智能体团队时，这一过程会进一步加速。我们的结果展示了一条实用且可扩展的路径，即将编码智能体部署到现实世界中自主推进机器人技术。

Original abstract: Achieving dexterous robotic manipulation in the real world heavily relies on human supervision and algorithm engineering, which becomes a central bottleneck in the pursuit of general physical intelligence. Although emerging coding agents can generate code to automate algorithm search, their successes remain largely confined in digital environments. We conjecture that the missing abstraction to automate robotics research is a repeatable feedback loop for real-world policy improvement: reset the scene, execute a policy, verify the outcome, and refine the next iteration. To bridge this gap, we introduce ENPIRE, a harness framework for coding agents that instantiates this physical feedback routine with four core modules: an Environment module (EN) for automatic reset and verification, a Policy Improvement module (PI) that launches policy refinement, a Rollout module (R) to evaluate policies with one or multiple physical robots operating in parallel, and an Evolution module (E) in which coding agents analyze logs, consult literature, improve training infrastructure and algorithm code to address failure modes. This closed-loop system transforms real-world manipulation learning into a controllable optimization procedure, minimizing human effort while allowing fair ablations across training recipe and agent variants. Powered by ENPIRE, frontier coding agents can autonomously train a policy to achieve a 99% success rate on challenging, dexterous manipulation tasks, such as organizing a pin box, fastening a zip tie, and tool use, a process that further accelerates when we dispatch an agent team on a robot fleet. Our results suggest a practical and scalable path toward deploying coding agents to autonomously advancing robotics in the physical world.

### [45] [Reward as An Agent for Embodied World Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19990v2)
*Pu Li,Zhigang Lin,Qiang Wu,Yongxuan Lv,Fei Wang,Shan You*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 奖励作为agent的框架，可缓解奖励黑客问题，通用agent方法。

TL;DR: 提出通过主动验证框架和多样化探索策略相结合，在具身世界模型中实现更可靠且可扩展的强化学习。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有强化学习方法在优化世界模型时过于保守，限制了探索和多样性；核心限制不是探索本身，而是缺乏可靠的验证策略来避免奖励黑客攻击。

Method: 引入“奖励即智能体”作为主动验证框架，提供稳健奖励并缓解分布偏移下的奖励黑客攻击；同时提出基于DynDiff-GRPO的动态感知rollout多样化，显式扩展动作空间探索以增加轨迹多样性。将两者统一实现可靠奖励基础上的多样化采样。

Result: 在多个开源世界模型中显著提升了准确率，并有效减轻了奖励黑客攻击。

Conclusion: 证明了当以稳健验证为基础时，更广泛的探索可以在强化学习中成功扩展。

中文摘要：虽然强化学习已成为完善世界模型的有前途的工具，但现有方法主要依赖于训练分布附近的保守 rollout，限制了探索、行为多样性和更丰富的动态发现。在这项工作中，我们挑战了这一保守范式。我们认为核心限制并非探索本身，而是缺乏支持更广泛探索的可靠验证策略。没有可靠的验证，扩展的探索极易受到奖励黑客攻击，即策略利用不完美的奖励而未能实现真正的改进。为了评估这一动机，我们将我们的方法实例化到具身世界模型中，其中物理合理性和任务完成提供了复杂动态下可扩展强化学习的严格测试平台。在验证方面，我们引入了“奖励即智能体”（Reward as an Agent），一种主动评估生成行为以提供稳健奖励信号并减轻分布偏移下奖励黑客攻击的智能体奖励框架。在探索方面，我们通过 DynDiff-GRPO 引入了动态感知的 rollout 多样化，它显式扩展动作空间探索以多样化轨迹、拓宽状态-动作覆盖范围，并鼓励超越保守 rollout 制度的更丰富具身行为。通过将“奖励即智能体”与 DynDiff-GRPO 统一，我们在更可靠的奖励基础上实现了具有大幅多样化采样的强化学习，有效减轻了奖励黑客攻击，同时在多个开源世界模型中取得了显著的准确率提升，从而证明了当以稳健验证为基础时，更广泛的探索可以成功扩展。

Original abstract: While RL has become a promising tool for refining world models, existing methods largely rely on conservative rollouts near the training distribution, limiting exploration, behavioral diversity, and richer dynamic discovery. In this work, we challenge this conservative paradigm. We argue that the core limitation is not exploration itself, but the lack of reliable verification strategies to support broader exploration. Without reliable verification, expanded exploration becomes highly susceptible to reward hacking, where policies exploit imperfect rewards without achieving genuine improvement. To evaluate this motivation, we instantiate our method in embodied world models, where physical plausibility, and task completion provide a rigorous testbed for scalable RL under complex dynamics. On the verification side, we introduce Reward as an Agent, an agentic reward framework that actively evaluates generated behaviors to provide robust reward signals and mitigate reward hacking under distribution shifts. On the exploration side, we introduce Dynamic-Aware Rollout Diversification through DynDiff-GRPO, which explicitly expands action-space exploration to diversify trajectories, broaden state-action coverage, and encourage richer embodied behaviors beyond conservative rollout regimes. By unifying Reward as an Agent with DynDiff-GRPO, we enable RL on a more reliable reward foundation with substantially diversified sampling, effectively mitigating reward hacking while yielding significant accuracy gains across multiple open-source world models, thereby demonstrating that broader exploration can scale successfully when grounded in robust verification.

### [46] [Autonomous Event-Driven Multi-Agent Orchestration for Enterprise AI at Scale](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20058v1)
*Harsh Rao Dhanyamraju,Leonidas Raghav,Aaron Lee*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 多agent编排框架，含事件驱动和优先级管理，通用架构。

TL;DR: 研究发现，多智能体系统在企业规模下性能下降的主要瓶颈是代理发现噪声，而非任务复杂度；提出的任务管理器通过优先级推理、事件合并和抢占显著降低了延迟并提升了正确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有多智能体系统大多假设离散请求-响应工作流，缺乏对企业规模下连续事件监控和行动的支持，且对企业级应用的研究不足。

Method: 在208个企业场景中评估DAG Plan and Execute和ReAct两种架构，并引入包含优先级推理、相关事件合并和抢占的任务管理器。

Result: 规模主导性能，简单任务下降更严重；DAG Plan and Execute在小规模精度高但开销大，ReAct更稳健；任务管理器将高优先级队列延迟降低14-75%，相关事件正确性提升超过20个百分点。

Conclusion: 企业规模下需关注代理发现噪声和连续操作机制，任务管理器是有效解决方案。

中文摘要：企业AI旨在朝着跨专家代理的持续事件监控、检测和行动发展，然而现有的多智能体系统大多假设离散的请求-响应工作流，并且在企业规模上仍未得到充分探索。我们评估了DAG Plan and Execute和ReAct在208个来自生产的企业场景中的表现，这些场景涵盖Persona（<10个智能体）、Department（20-80个）和Enterprise（200个）规模，并引入了任务管理器，通过优先级推理、相关事件合并和抢占实现持续操作。结果表明，主导编排性能的是规模而非任务复杂度：两种架构在小规模下表现良好，但在企业规模下，随着代理发现噪声成为主要瓶颈，性能下降，简单任务比复杂任务下降得更严重。DAG Plan and Execute在较小规模下提供更高的精度和结构化并行化，但其更高的开销在企业规模下恶化；ReAct通过增量处理故障更为稳健。任务管理器在企业规模下将高优先级队列延迟降低了14-75%，并将相关事件正确性提高了超过20个百分点。

Original abstract: Enterprise AI aims to move toward continuous event monitoring, detection, and action across specialist agents, yet existing multi-agent systems largely assume discrete request-response workflows and remain underexplored at enterprise scale. We evaluate DAG Plan and Execute and ReAct across 208 production-derived enterprise scenarios spanning Persona (<10 agents), Department (20-80), and Enterprise (200) scales, and introduce a Task Manager for continuous operation via priority inference, related-event merging, and preemption. Results show that scale, not task complexity, dominates orchestration performance: both architectures perform well at small scale but degrade at enterprise scale as agent discovery noise becomes the primary bottleneck, with simple tasks degrading more sharply than complex ones. DAG Plan and Execute offers higher precision and structured parallelization at smaller scales, but its higher overhead worsens at enterprise scale; ReAct is more robust by handling failures incrementally. The Task Manager reduces high-priority queue latency by 14-75% and improves related-event correctness by over 20 percentage points at enterprise scale.

### [47] [Process-Verified Reinforcement Learning for Theorem Proving via Lean](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20068v1)
*Minsu Kim,Se-Young Yun*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 过程验证RL用于定理证明，结构化反馈可迁移至代码优化验证。

TL;DR: 本文利用Lean证明助手提供细粒度的策略级验证反馈，通过GRPO风格强化学习目标结合首次错误传播，显著提升了形式推理性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RLVR仅依赖二元信号，缺乏过程级监督；而符号证明助手能提供丰富结构化反馈，但未被充分利用来产生密集、可靠的奖励信号。

Method: 将证明解析为策略序列，利用Lean的精化过程标记正确与错误步骤，生成基于类型论的信用信号；纳入GRPO目标，采用首次错误传播和首个令牌信用方法平衡结果与过程级优势。

Result: 在STP-Lean和DeepSeek-Prover-V1.5上实验，策略级监督在多数设置下优于仅结果基线，在MiniF2F和ProofNet等基准上取得改进。

Conclusion: 符号证明助手可作为过程级奖励预言机，将语言模型可扩展性与符号验证可靠性结合，为形式推理强化学习提供新路径。

中文摘要：尽管基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）通常依赖于单一的二元验证信号，但形式推理中的符号证明助手提供了丰富、细粒度的结构化反馈。结构化过程与非结构化奖励之间的这种差距凸显了既密集又可靠的反馈的重要性。在这项工作中，我们演示了Lean证明助手本身可以作为符号过程预言机，在训练期间提供结果级别和细粒度的策略级别验证反馈。证明尝试被解析为策略序列，Lean的精化过程标记出局部正确的步骤和最早出错的步骤，从而产生基于类型论的密集、验证器支持的信用信号。我们将这些结构化奖励纳入GRPO风格的强化学习目标中，并采用首次错误传播和首个令牌信用方法，平衡结果级别和过程级别的优势。使用STP-Lean和DeepSeek-Prover-V1.5的实验表明，在大多数设置中，策略级别监督优于仅结果基线，在MiniF2F和ProofNet等基准测试上带来了改进。除了实证收益，我们的研究还强调了更广阔的视角：符号证明助手不仅在评估时是验证器，还可以在训练期间充当过程级别的奖励预言机。这为强化学习框架开辟了一条路径，将语言模型的可扩展性与符号验证的可靠性相结合，用于形式推理。

Original abstract: While reinforcement learning from verifiable rewards (RLVR) typically has relied on a single binary verification signal, symbolic proof assistants in formal reasoning offer rich, fine-grained structured feedback. This gap between structured processes and unstructured rewards highlights the importance of feedback that is both dense and sound. In this work, we demonstrate that the Lean proof assistant itself can serve as a symbolic process oracle, supplying both outcome-level and fine-grained tactic-level verified feedback during training. Proof attempts are parsed into tactic sequences, and Lean's elaboration marks both locally sound steps and the earliest failing step, yielding dense, verifier-grounded credit signals rooted in type theory. We incorporate these structured rewards into a GRPO-style reinforcement learning objective with first-error propagation and first-token credit methods that balances outcome- and process-level advantages. Experiments with STP-Lean and DeepSeek-Prover-V1.5 show that tactic-level supervision outperforms outcome-only baselines in most settings, delivering improvements on benchmarks such as MiniF2F and ProofNet. Beyond empirical gains, our study highlights a broader perspective: symbolic proof assistants are not only verifiers at evaluation time, but can also act as process-level reward oracles during training. This opens a path toward reinforcement learning frameworks that combine the scalability of language models with the reliability of symbolic verification for formal reasoning.

</details>


### [48] [ScaffoldAgent: Utility-Guided Dynamic Outline Optimization for Open-Ended Deep Research](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20122v1)
*Zhibang Yang,Xinke Jiang,Yuzhen Xiao,Ruizhe Zhang,Yue Fang,XinFei Wan,Zhengxing Song,Yuxuan Liu,Yuheng Huang,Xu Chu,Junfeng Zhao,Yasha Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出效用引导的动态大纲优化框架，用于开放研究，包含扩展/收缩/修订操作和效用反馈，可迁移到代码agent的结构优化。

TL;DR: 提出ScaffoldAgent框架，通过动态大纲优化（扩展、收缩、修改）和实用导向反馈机制，解决了开放式深度研究中的大纲漂移问题，提升了长篇报告生成质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在开放式深度研究中固定大纲或仅局部修改，导致信息积累时大纲漂移以及修改评估延迟。

Method: 将大纲演化建模为结构化决策过程（扩展、收缩、修改），并引入实用导向反馈机制，结合检索增益、结构连贯性和试生成质量来指导操作选择和终止。

Result: 在DeepResearch Bench和DeepResearch Gym上，ScaffoldAgent在长篇报告生成和事实基础方面优于现有深度研究智能体。

Conclusion: ScaffoldAgent通过动态优化大纲有效提升了开放式深度研究的报告生成质量。

中文摘要：开放式深度研究（OEDR）要求系统通过多轮检索获取知识并生成连贯的长篇报告。大纲作为结构骨架起着核心作用，协调检索、证据组织和生成。然而，现有方法要么在写作前固定大纲，要么使用局部启发式方法进行修改，导致在持续信息积累下的骨架漂移，以及评估大纲修改的延迟反馈。我们提出ScaffoldAgent，一种用于OEDR的实用导向动态大纲优化框架。ScaffoldAgent将大纲演化建模为具有三种操作的结构化决策过程：扩展、收缩和修改，从而实现对报告骨架的受控更新。它进一步引入了一种实用导向的反馈机制，通过检索收益、结构连贯性和试生成质量来估计每个大纲操作的下游价值。由此产生的实用信号指导推理过程中的节点选择、操作调度和终止。在DeepResearch Bench和DeepResearch Gym上的实验表明，ScaffoldAgent在长篇报告生成和事实基础方面持续优于现有的深度研究智能体。

Original abstract: Open-ended deep research (OEDR) requires systems to acquire knowledge through multi-round retrieval and generate coherent long-form reports. The outline plays a central role as a structural scaffold that coordinates retrieval, evidence organization, and generation. However, existing methods either fix the outline before writing or refine it with local heuristics, leading to scaffold drift under continuous information accumulation and delayed feedback for evaluating outline modifications. We propose ScaffoldAgent, a utility-guided dynamic outline optimization framework for OEDR. ScaffoldAgent models outline evolution as a structured decision process with three operations: Expansion, Contraction, and Revision, enabling controlled updates to the report scaffold. It further introduces a utility-guided feedback mechanism that estimates the downstream value of each outline operation from retrieval gain, structural coherence, and trial-generation quality. The resulting utility signal guides node selection, operation scheduling, and termination during inference. Experiments on DeepResearch Bench and DeepResearch Gym show that ScaffoldAgent consistently improves long-form report generation and factual grounding over existing deep research agents.

### [49] [RACL: Reasoning-Agent Control Layers for Continuous Metaheuristic Learning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20142v1)
*Antón Asla Manzárraga*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出推理agent层控制元启发式优化，通过观察、推理、干预、验证和策略巩固，直接可迁移到代码优化agent中的搜索控制。

TL;DR: 提出RACL方法，通过推理代理控制元启发式算法内部搜索，在车辆路径问题中显著提升性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有元启发式优化器缺乏对内部搜索行为的智能控制，需要一种能自动发现和验证控制规则的方法。

Method: RACL在优化器上添加推理代理，通过观察操作内存、推理历史行为、提出有界假设、测试干预并评估结果，结合护栏和解释机制来动态调整搜索策略。

Result: 在21个可行案例中，RACL在21个中优于或持平OMP，18个中优于或持平STP；平均成本比STP低0.641%；在Sevilla-9/10样本中，比Fixed低8.337%，比STP低1.605%，且计算开销可忽略。

Conclusion: RACL方法能有效让推理代理发现、验证并应用控制规则，提升元启发式算法性能，且具有可解释性和可重复性。

中文摘要：本文介绍了RACL，一种用于元启发式算法的推理代理控制层。RACL将一个推理代理置于现有优化器之上。该代理不替代优化器，也不修改业务约束。相反，它通过观察操作内存、推理过去行为、制定有界假设、测试干预、评估结果、应用护栏、巩固有用策略并解释其决策来控制优化器的内部搜索行为。实验使用车辆路径规划作为测试平台，但贡献不是新的路由求解器、特定的ALNS配置或特定的路由规则集。贡献在于RACL方法：一种推理代理为元启发式算法发现、验证、巩固和解释算法控制规则的方式。在当前实验设置中，RACL在21个可行案例中的21个中改善或持平了操作内存策略，在21个可行案例中的18个中改善或持平了非推理停滞触发策略，平均RACL与STP成本差为-0.641%。在Sevilla-9/10运行时样本中，与Fixed相比，RACL平均成本改善了-8.337%，与STP相比改善了-1.605%，且未显示实质性计算开销。在概念验证期间，Codex被用作循环推理代理，观察执行、解释日志并提出实时有界干预。策略代理后仅用于使定量评估可重复。

Original abstract: This paper introduces RACL, a Reasoning-Agent Control Layer for metaheuristics. RACL places a reasoning agent above an existing optimizer. The agent does not replace the optimizer and does not modify business constraints. Instead, it controls the optimizer's internal search behavior by observing operational memory, reasoning over past behavior, formulating bounded hypotheses, testing interventions, evaluating outcomes, applying guardrails, consolidating useful policies and explaining its decisions. The experiment uses vehicle routing as a testbed, but the contribution is not a new routing solver, a particular ALNS configuration or a specific set of routing rules. The contribution is the RACL method: a way for a reasoning agent to discover, validate, consolidate and explain algorithmic control rules for a metaheuristic. In the current experimental setting, RACL improves or ties the Operational Memory Policy in 21 of 21 feasible cases and improves or ties a non-reasoning Stagnation-Triggered Policy in 18 of 21 feasible cases, with an average RACL vs STP cost delta of -0.641%. In the Sevilla-9/10 runtime sample, RACL improves average cost by -8.337% versus Fixed and -1.605% versus STP without showing material computational overhead. During the proof-of-concept, Codex was used as an in-the-loop reasoning agent observing executions, interpreting logs and proposing live bounded interventions. The policy proxy was later used only to make quantitative evaluation reproducible.

### [50] [QMFOL: Benchmarking Large Language Model Reasoning via Quantifiable Monadic First-Order Logic Test Case Generation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20227v1)
*Xinyi Zheng,Ling Shi,Tianlong Yu,Yongxin Zhao,Lorenz Goette,Kailong Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出QMFOL框架自动生成可控复杂性的演绎推理任务，构建QMFOLBench基准，评估发现逻辑复杂性降低模型性能，且模型对标签类型和语义变化敏感。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准缺乏对逻辑复杂性的细粒度控制，且在平衡语义多样性与逻辑一致性方面存在困难。

Method: 使用合取和析取模式构建形式逻辑结构，精确控制推理深度、宽度、标签类型和干扰项；通过LLM将结构转化为自然语言，并利用外部证明器进行往返验证以确保逻辑一致性。

Result: 构建QMFOLBench基准（2880实例，960配置），对六个LRMs和两个LLMs的评估显示：性能随逻辑复杂度增加而下降，计算开销增加；模型在True标签任务上优于False/Unknown，且对语义变化敏感。

Conclusion: QMFOL提供了可扩展且可靠的方法来构建可控复杂性的演绎推理基准，从而更精确地评估现代语言模型的推理能力。

中文摘要：大语言模型（LLMs）在推理方面取得了显著进展，尤其是在演绎推理方面，这对高风险决策至关重要。随着模型的改进，评估基准也应随之发展。然而，现有基准缺乏对逻辑复杂性的细粒度控制，并且在平衡语义多样性和逻辑一致性方面存在困难。为了解决这些问题，我们提出了QMFOL，一个自动生成具有可量化和可控复杂性的单子一阶逻辑推理任务的框架。它使用合取和析取模式构建形式逻辑结构，从而能够精确控制推理深度、宽度、标签类型和干扰项。然后，这些结构通过LLMs转化为自然语言，并通过使用外部证明器的往返验证确保逻辑一致性。基于我们的框架，我们构建了QMFOLBench，一个包含2880个实例、960种配置的基准，涵盖不同的逻辑和语义维度。对六个大型推理模型（LRMs）和两个LLMs的评估表明，随着逻辑复杂性的增加，性能下降且计算开销增加。模型在True标签任务上的表现优于False或Unknown标签任务，并且对语义变化敏感。总体而言，QMFOL提供了一种可扩展且可靠的方法，用于构建具有可控复杂性的演绎推理基准，从而能够更精确地评估现代语言模型的推理能力。

Original abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) have made significant progress in reasoning, particularly in deductive reasoning, which is crucial for high-stakes decision-making. As models improve, evaluation benchmarks should evolve to keep pace. However, existing benchmarks lack fine-grained control over logical complexity and struggle to balance semantic diversity with logical consistency.
  To address these issues, we propose QMFOL, an automated framework for generating monadic first-order logic reasoning tasks with quantifiable and controllable complexity. It constructs formal logical structures using conjunction and disjunction patterns, enabling precise control over reasoning depth, width, label types, and distractors. These structures are then translated into natural language via LLMs, with logical consistency ensured through round-trip verification using an external prover. Based on our framework, we build QMFOLBench, a benchmark comprising 2880 instances with 960 configurations across diverse logical and semantic dimensions. Evaluations on six large reasoning models (LRMs) and two LLMs show that performance degrades and computational overhead increases with rising logical complexity. Models perform better on True-labeled tasks than on False or Unknown ones, and exhibit sensitivity to semantic variation. Overall, QMFOL offers a scalable and reliable approach for constructing deductive reasoning benchmarks with controllable complexity, enabling more precise evaluation of reasoning capabilities in modern language models.

### [51] [A Multi-Agent system for Multi-Objective constrained optimization](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20236v1)
*Federica Filippini*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 多agent系统用于多目标约束优化，通用多agent协作方法可迁移至coding agent团队

TL;DR: MAMO通过多智能体强化学习自动学习奖励权重，以平衡约束优化中的成本与约束违反。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法手动选择奖励权重，难以在动态环境中平衡优化目标与约束违反。

Method: 提出MAMO框架，利用多智能体强化学习将奖励权重的选择作为学习问题，解耦任务执行与目标设计。

Result: 实现了更自主和鲁棒的约束优化，初步验证了方法的有效性。

Conclusion: MAMO为动态环境中约束优化问题的自主RL解决方案提供了新思路。

中文摘要：许多计算和网络系统中的决策问题可以自然地表述为在性能约束下的成本最小化问题。在动态环境中，强化学习（RL）常被用于运行时解决此类问题，通过加权惩罚项将成本和约束违反嵌入到单个标量奖励中，遵循拉格朗日启发式的公式。然而，在这种情况下，学习策略的行为关键取决于这些权重的选择，而权重通常是手动选择的。这使得难以在优化主要目标和有效避免约束违反之间找到适当的权衡，尤其是在非平稳环境中，它们的相对重要性可能会发生变化。本文提出了MAMO（多智能体系统用于多目标约束优化），一种通过多智能体RL解决这一平衡问题的方法。MAMO将任务执行与目标设计解耦，将奖励权重的选择制定为一个学习问题，为动态环境中约束优化问题的更自主和鲁棒的基于RL的解决方案迈出了第一步。

Original abstract: Many decision-making problems in computing and networking systems can be naturally formulated as cost-minimization problems under performance constraints. In dynamic environments, reinforcement learning (RL) is often used to solve such problems at runtime by embedding both costs and constraint violations into a single scalar reward through weighted penalty terms, following a Lagrangian-inspired formulation. However, in this context the behavior of the learned policy critically depends on the choice of these weights, which are typically selected manually. This makes it difficult to identify an appropriate trade-off between optimizing the primary objective and effectively avoiding constraint violations, particularly in non-stationary environments where their relative importance may change. This paper presents MAMO (Multi-Agent system for Multi-Objective constrained optimization), an approach to tackle this balancing problem through multi-agent RL. MAMO decouples task execution from objective design by formulating the selection of reward weights as a learning problem, providing a !rst step towards more autonomous and robust RL-based solutions for constrained optimization problems in dynamic environments.

### [52] [Navigating Unreliable Parametric and Contextual Knowledge: Explicit Knowledge Conflict Resolution for LLM Inference](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20245v1)
*Huang Peng,Jiuyang Tang,Weixin Zeng,Hao Xu,Xiang Zhao*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 多agent推理框架解决知识冲突，通用推理和冲突解决机制可迁移至代码优化agent

TL;DR: 提出MACR框架，通过多智能体推理显式解决LLM中的知识冲突，显著提升性能并提供可解释性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法假设模型或外部知识可靠，忽略双方可能出错，且缺乏主动解决冲突机制。

Method: 先自适应评估知识置信度（基于语义熵），选择内部知识外化或外部检索生成基础上下文；再用三个智能体分别归纳规则、分析冲突、解决不一致。

Result: 在多个基准上显著优于SOTA基线，并提供显式冲突的可解释解决方案。

Conclusion: MACR有效解决知识冲突，具备可解释性，是一种优于二元选择范式的新方法。

中文摘要：大语言模型（LLMs）通过利用广泛的参数知识和上下文学习能力，在广泛的语言任务上取得了强大的性能，使其能够整合输入提示中提供的外部信息。然而，外部知识的整合可能引入冲突，不仅在于模型内部参数知识与外部信息之间，还在于多个外部上下文之间。现有方法通常假设模型或提供的上下文是可靠的，忽视了两种来源都可能包含错误的可能性，并通过优先考虑一个来源来避免冲突，而不是主动解决不一致。为了解决这些局限，我们提出了一个新颖的框架MACR，用于LLM知识冲突解决，超越了传统的二元选择范式，并基于多智能体推理方法引入了显式的冲突解决机制。具体来说，我们首先提出了一种自适应知识评估和检索方法，采用修改的语义熵度量来量化LLM对给定查询答案的置信度。基于此置信度估计，MACR要么将模型的内部知识外化为文本表示，要么在内部知识不足时检索相关外部知识，生成用于后续推理的基础上下文。然后，我们引入了一个归纳的多智能体推理框架，包含三个专门智能体，分别归纳显式规则、分析潜在冲突以及解决所有可用上下文中的不一致。实验结果表明，MACR在多个基准测试中显著优于最先进的基线，同时提供了显式冲突的可解释解决方案。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have achieved strong performance across a wide range of language-based tasks by leveraging both extensive parametric knowledge and in-context learning ability, enabling them to incorporate external information provided in the input prompt. However, the integration of external knowledge can introduce conflicts, not only between the model's internal parametric knowledge and the external information, but also among multiple pieces of external contexts. Existing approaches typically assume that either the model or the provided context is reliable, overlooking the possibility that both sources may contain errors, and avoid conflicts by privileging one source over the other, rather than actively resolving inconsistencies. To address these limitations, we propose a novel framework MACR for LLM knowledge conflict resolution that moves beyond the conventional binary choice paradigm and incorporates an explicit conflict-resolution mechanism based on a multi-agent reasoning approach. Specifically, we first propose an adaptive knowledge assessment and retrieval approach that employs a modified semantic entropy measure to quantify an LLM's confidence in its answer to a given query. Based on this confidence estimation, MACR either externalizes the model's internal knowledge as textual representations or retrieves relevant external knowledge when internal knowledge is insufficient, generating basic contexts for subsequent reasoning. Then we introduce an inductive multi-agent reasoning framework with three specialized agents that, respectively, induce explicit rules, analyze potential conflicts, and resolve inconsistencies across all available contexts. Empirical results demonstrate that MACR significantly outperforms state-of-the-art baselines across benchmarks, while also providing interpretable resolutions of explicit conflicts.

</details>


### [53] [SoftSkill: Behavioral Compression for Contextual Adaptation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20333v1)
*Xijia Tao,Yihua Teng,Xinyu Fu,Ziru Liu,Kecheng Chen,Yuzhi Zhao,Suiyun Zhang,Rui Liu,Lingpeng Kong*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统以Markdown文件形式的自然语言技能需要模型在推理时重新解释长文本，效率低下且不灵活，因此探索是否能用紧凑的连续向量表示技能，并通过微调优化。

Result: 在单轮设置中，长度32的SoftSkill前缀在Qwen3.5-4B上相比无技能提示提升显著：SearchQA+8.3%，LiveMath+42.1%，DocVQA+1.3%；相比SkillOpt，SearchQA+5.2%，LiveMath+12.5%，且用少量虚拟标记替代大量Markdown标记。

Conclusion: 技能可作为紧凑的潜在控制而不是可读的Markdown，在冻结模型上通过软技能前缀实现更优性能，但对长程行为压缩仍具挑战。

中文摘要：智能体的技能通常以自然语言的Markdown文件形式部署，这些文件编码了回答策略、证据使用习惯和任务流程。这些文件可读且可移植，但它们是间接消耗的：对于每个任务实例，冻结的语言模型必须将长文本工件转换为生成时的行为。本文探讨了是否可以用自然语言技能来初始化一个紧凑的连续上下文对象，通过可训练的软增量进行精炼，同时保持基础模型冻结。我们提出了SoftSkill，一种冻结骨干的方法，该方法通过下一个标记预测来微调这种软技能，并在推理时将其作为潜在的行为先验部署。在我们的主要单轮设置中，在Qwen3.5-4B上使用长度为32的SoftSkill前缀，相比无技能提示，在SearchQA上提高了8.3个百分点，在LiveMath上提高了42.1个百分点，在DocVQA上提高了1.3个百分点。相对于SkillOpt，SoftSkill在SearchQA上准确率提高了5.2个百分点，在LiveMath上提高了12.5个百分点，同时用几个虚拟标记取代了成百上千个Markdown技能标记。我们进一步研究了作为更难边界情况的自主执行，其中稀疏轨迹模仿提供了有用的信号，但尚未稳健地压缩长程程序性行为。更广泛地说，结果表明，一些任务技能最好不被视为推理时需要重新解释的额外Markdown，而是作为冻结模型进入任务时的紧凑潜在控制。

Original abstract: Agent skills are commonly deployed as natural-language Markdown files that encode answer policies, evidence-use habits, and task procedures. These files are readable and portable, but they are consumed indirectly: for each task instance, a frozen language model must translate a long textual artifact into generation-time behavior. This paper asks whether a natural-language skill can instead initialize a compact continuous context object, refined by a trainable soft delta while the base model remains frozen. We propose SoftSkill, a frozen-backbone method that tunes such soft skills with next-token prediction and deploys them as latent behavioral priors at inference time. In our main single-round setting, a length-32 SoftSkill prefix on Qwen3.5-4B improves over no-skill prompting by 8.3 points on SearchQA, 42.1 points on LiveMath, and 1.3 points on DocVQA. Relative to SkillOpt, SoftSkill improves accuracy by 5.2 points on SearchQA and 12.5 points on LiveMath, while replacing hundreds to thousands of Markdown skill tokens with a few virtual tokens. We further study agentic execution as a harder boundary case, where sparse trajectory imitation provides useful signal but does not yet robustly compress long-horizon procedural behavior. More broadly, the results suggest that some task skills are better treated not as additional Markdown to be reinterpreted at inference time, but as compact latent controls over how a frozen model enters the task.

</details>


### [54] [Automating SKILL.md Generation for Computer-Using Agents via Interaction Trajectory Mining](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20363v1)
*Yuexing Hao,Xiaomin Li*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 从交互轨迹挖掘技能库，可迁移到coding agent的技能复用与规划

TL;DR: 轨迹挖掘可提取可读技能库，但跨域策略改进不足。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究是否可以从交互数据中挖掘技能库以改进下游策略。

Method: 三阶段流水线：分割GUI轨迹、聚类片段、训练技能感知策略。

Result: 聚类纯度高达0.95，但技能感知策略仅将IW步骤准确率从18.5%提升至20.5%，BrowseComp+无明显变化，且低于简单频率先验。

Conclusion: 轨迹挖掘可暴露技能结构，但当前边界检测、表示和奖励模型不足以支撑可靠跨域策略改进。

中文摘要：明确的技能库使计算机使用代理更易于检查，但目前尚不清楚是否可以从交互数据中挖掘出这样的库，从而改进下游策略。我们通过一个三阶段流水线研究这个问题：分割GUI轨迹，将片段聚类为候选技能，并根据生成的注释训练一个技能感知的策略。挖掘出的聚类在源基准上是可读的：八个聚类中有五个与InteraSkill Workflows标签的纯度至少为0.95。然而，可读性并不意味着可迁移。GRPO仅将IW技能步骤准确率从18.5%提高到20.5%，使BrowseComp+基本保持不变，并在关键源域指标上低于简单的频率先验。因此，我们将该方法作为一项诊断研究：轨迹挖掘可以暴露可检查的技能结构，但当前的边界检测器、无序片段表示和离线奖励模型不足以实现可靠的跨域策略改进。

Original abstract: Explicit skill libraries make computer-using agents easier to inspect, but it remains unclear whether such libraries can be mined from interaction data in a way that improves downstream policies. We study this question through a three-stage pipeline that segments GUI trajectories, clusters segments into candidate skills, and trains a skill-aware policy from the resulting annotations. The mined clusters are readable on the source benchmark: five of eight clusters have at least 0.95 purity against InteraSkill Workflows labels. However, readability does not imply transfer. GRPO improves IW skill-step accuracy only from 18.5\% to 20.5\%, leaves BrowseComp+ essentially unchanged, and underperforms trivial frequency priors on key source-domain metrics. We therefore present the method as a diagnostic study: trajectory mining can expose inspectable skill structure, but the current boundary detector, orderless segment representation, and offline reward model are insufficient for reliable cross-domain policy improvement.

### [55] [What Do Safety-Aligned LLMs Learn From Mixed Compliance Demonstrations?](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20508v1)
*Sihui Dai,Mann Patel*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 研究上下文演示如何影响LLM安全行为，可迁移至agent安全控制

TL;DR: 研究了上下文示范中良性和有害合规示范对模型有害行为的影响，发现它们的不可互换性、偏好优化的关键作用、近因偏差以及模型间的差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前工作表明示范可破解模型，但不清楚模型如何理解不同类型的合规示范，因此需要探究示范组成如何驱动有害合规。

Method: 混合良性和有害合规示范，测试三种假设，在四个模型上进行实验，分析示范内容、排序和训练方法的影响。

Result: 良性和有害示范不可互换；良性示范可减少或增加有害合规；偏好优化是防止良性示范增加有害合规的关键；排序有近因偏差；模型在拒绝时对上下文信号的处理方式不同。

Conclusion: 模型从合规示范中提取的内容依赖于示范内容、排序和训练方法，揭示了示范破解的工作机制。

中文摘要：先前的研究表明，上下文中的示范可以破解语言模型，但模型如何解读不同类型的合规示范仍不清楚。我们通过将良性合规示范（无害请求，有用响应）与有害合规示范（有害请求，有用响应）混合，并测试关于示范组成如何驱动有害合规的三种假设来研究这一点。在四个模型中，我们发现良性和有害示范不可互换：良性示范根据模型的不同可能减少或增加有害合规。我们进一步表明，偏好优化是防止良性示范增加有害合规的关键训练阶段，示范排序表现出强烈的近因偏差，并且模型在拒绝与上下文学习的交互方式上存在差异：有些模型在拒绝时仍采用示范格式，而另一些模型则在拒绝时覆盖所有上下文信号。综合来看，这项工作超越了展示基于示范的破解有效性的层面，转向描述其工作机制：模型从合规示范中提取的内容取决于示范内容、排序和训练方法。

Original abstract: Prior work has shown that in-context demonstrations can jailbreak language models, but it remains unclear how models interpret different types of compliance demonstrations. We study this by mixing benign compliance demonstrations (non-harmful request, helpful response) with harmful compliance demonstrations (harmful request, helpful response) and testing three hypotheses about how demonstration composition drives harmful compliance. Across four models, we find that benign and harmful demonstrations are not interchangeable: benign demonstrations can either reduce or increase harmful compliance depending on the model. We further show that preference optimization is the critical training stage that prevents benign demonstrations from increasing harmful compliance, that demonstration ordering exhibits strong recency bias, and that models differ in how refusal interacts with in-context learning: some adopt demonstrated formatting even when refusing, while others override all in-context signals upon refusal. Taken together, this work moves beyond showing that demonstration-based jailbreaking works to characterizing how it works: what models extract from compliance demonstrations depends on demonstration content, ordering, and training methodology.

### [56] [Multi-LCB: Extending LiveCodeBench to Multiple Programming Languages](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20517v1)
*Maria Ivanova,Pavel Zadorozhny,Rodion Levichev,Ivan Petrov,Adamenko Pavel,Ivan Lopatin,Alexey Kutalev,Dmitrii Babaev*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 多语言代码生成基准，直接评估coding agent跨语言能力

TL;DR: 提出Multi-LCB基准，扩展LCB至12种编程语言，发现LLM存在Python过拟合和多语言性能差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LCB仅限于Python，无法评估LLM跨语言代码生成能力。

Method: 将LCB中Python任务转换为其他11种语言，保持污染控制和评估协议，自动跟踪更新。

Result: 评估24个LLM，发现Python过拟合、语言特定污染和多语言性能差异。

Conclusion: Multi-LCB成为多语言代码评估的新基准，暴露了LLM的关键能力差距。

中文摘要：LiveCodeBench (LCB) 最近已成为评估大型语言模型（LLM）在代码生成任务上的广泛采用的基准。通过策划竞争性编程问题、不断向集合中添加新问题并按发布日期进行过滤，LCB提供了污染感知的评估，并提供了编码能力的整体视图。然而，LCB仍然局限于Python，留下了LLM是否能泛化到现实软件工程所需的各种编程语言的问题。我们引入了Multi-LCB，这是一个用于评估LLM跨十二种编程语言（包括Python）的基准。Multi-LCB将LCB数据集中的Python任务转换为其他语言的等效任务，同时保留LCB的污染控制和评估协议。由于它与原始LCB格式完全兼容，Multi-LCB将自动跟踪未来的LCB更新，从而实现跨语言代码生成能力的系统评估，并要求模型在Python之外保持性能。我们评估了24个LLM在Multi-LCB上的指令和推理能力，发现了Python过拟合、语言特定污染以及多语言性能显著差异的证据。我们的结果将Multi-LCB确立为多编程语言代码评估的严格新基准，直接解决了LCB的主要局限性，并暴露了当前LLM能力的关键差距。

Original abstract: LiveCodeBench (LCB) has recently become a widely adopted benchmark for evaluating large language models (LLMs) on code-generation tasks. By curating competitive programming problems, constantly adding fresh problems to the set, and filtering them by release dates, LCB provides contamination-aware evaluation and offers a holistic view of coding capability. However, LCB remains restricted to Python, leaving open the question of whether LLMs can generalize across the diverse programming languages required in real-world software engineering.
  We introduce Multi-LCB, a benchmark for evaluating LLMs across twelve programming languages, including Python. Multi-LCB transforms Python tasks from the LCB dataset into equivalent tasks in other languages while preserving LCB's contamination controls and evaluation protocol. Because it is fully compatible with the original LCB format, Multi-LCB will automatically track future LCB updates, enabling systematic assessment of cross-language code generation competence and requiring models to sustain performance well beyond Python.
  We evaluated 24 LLMs for instruction and reasoning on Multi-LCB, uncovering evidence of Python overfitting, language-specific contamination, and substantial disparities in multilingual performance. Our results establish Multi-LCB as a rigorous new benchmark for multi-programming-language code evaluation, directly addressing LCB's primary limitation and exposing critical gaps in current LLM capabilities.

### [57] [LedgerAgent: Structured State for Policy-Adherent Tool-Calling Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20529v1)
*Md Nayem Uddin,Amir Saeidi,Eduardo Blanco,Chitta Baral*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出显式状态管理的工具调用agent方法，对coding agent的policy adherence有启发。

TL;DR: LedgerAgent通过维护任务状态账本并渲染到提示中，改善了工具调用代理的策略遵从性，在多个领域和模型上提升了pass^k指标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准工具调用代理中任务状态管理隐式，导致代理基于过时或错误信息决策，且工具调用可能违反依赖当前状态的策略。

Method: 提出LedgerAgent，通过单独的账本维护观察到的任务状态，并将状态渲染到提示中，同时在执行环境改变的工具调用前检查状态相关的策略约束。

Result: 在四个客户服务领域和多种模型上，LedgerAgent相比标准方法提高了平均pass^k，尤其在更严格的多轮一致性指标下增益最大。

Conclusion: LedgerAgent通过显式状态管理和策略检查有效减少了状态相关错误，提升了工具调用代理的可靠性和策略遵从性。

中文摘要：在客户服务领域中，遵循策略的工具调用代理必须在对话轮次之间维护任务状态，同时调用工具并遵守领域策略。任务状态由通过用户交互和工具调用观察到的相关事实、标识符、约束和条件组成。在标准代理中，任务状态没有单独表示。观察结果、工具返回值和策略指令被放入提示中，使得代理每次决定下一步操作时都需要从提示中重建相关状态。这种设计使状态管理变得隐式，导致了两种常见的失败模式：代理可能检索到正确的事实，但随后将其决策基于过时、缺失或错误的信息；并且语法上有效的工具调用可能仍然违反依赖于当前任务状态的领域策略。我们引入了LedgerAgent，这是一种用于工具调用代理的推理时方法，它在单独的账本中维护观察到的任务状态，并将这些状态渲染到提示中。该账本还用于在执行改变环境的工具调用之前检查依赖于状态的策略约束，从而阻止策略违规。在四个客户服务领域以及混合的开放和封闭权重模型面板上，LedgerAgent相比标准的基于提示的工具调用方法提高了平均pass^k，在更严格的多轮一致性指标下改进最大。

Original abstract: Policy-adherent tool-calling agents in customer-service domains must maintain task states across turns while calling tools and obeying domain policies. Task states consist of relevant facts, identifiers, constraints, and conditions observed through user interaction and tool calls. In standard agents, task states are not represented separately. Observations, tool returns, and policy instructions are placed in the prompt, leaving agents to reconstruct the relevant states from the prompt each time they decide what to do next. This design makes state management implicit, creating two common failure modes. An agent may retrieve the right facts but later ground its decision in stale, missing, or incorrect information; and a syntactically valid tool call may still violate a domain policy that depends on the current task state. We introduce \textsc{LedgerAgent}, an inference-time method for tool-calling agents that maintains observed task states in a separate ledger and renders the states into the prompt. The ledger is also used to check state-dependent policy constraints before environment-changing tool calls are executed, blocking policy violations. Across four customer-service domains and a mixed panel of open- and closed-weight models, \textsc{LedgerAgent} improves average pass\textasciicircum{}k over a standard prompt-based tool-calling approach, with the largest gains under stricter multi-trial consistency metrics.

</details>


### [58] [Fara-1.5: Scalable Learning Environments for Computer Use Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20785v1)
*Ahmed Awadallah,Sahil Gupta,Yash Lara,Yadong Lu,Hussein Mozannar,Akshay Nambi,Zach Nussbaum,Yash Pandya,Aravind Rajeswaran,Corby Rosset,Alexey Taymanov,Luiz do Valle,Vibhav Vineet,Spencer Whitehead,Andrew Zhao*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出计算机使用agent的可扩展训练数据流水线，包括环境、解算器和验证器，对agent训练有方法论贡献。

TL;DR: 提出了FaraGen1.5可扩展数据流水线，用于生成计算机使用智能体的训练数据，并训练出Fara1.5系列模型，在浏览器使用基准上达到新的最先进水平。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 从人类演示中收集计算机使用数据昂贵且缓慢，需要可扩展的生成策略。

Method: 提出FaraGen1.5数据流水线，包含环境、求解器和验证器三个模块，使用实时网站和合成环境，结合多种模型和用户模拟器生成轨迹，并通过监督微调（SFT）训练Fara1.5模型。

Result: Fara1.5-9B在Online-Mind2Web上达63.4%，WebVoyager上达86.6%；Fara1.5-27B在Online-Mind2Web上达72.3%，与更大专有系统竞争。

Conclusion: 每个规模类别的Fara1.5模型在浏览器使用基准上均达到新的最先进水平。

中文摘要：从人类演示中收集计算机使用数据既昂贵又缓慢，这激发了对可扩展生成策略的需求。这需要两个关键要素：智能体可以行动的环境，以及可以判断其演示是否成功的验证器。我们引入了FaraGen1.5，这是一个用于计算机使用智能体的可扩展数据流水线，由三个模块化组件组成：环境、求解器和验证器。FaraGen1.5同时使用实时网站和合成环境，这些合成环境忠实地模拟了需要认证或需要不可逆操作的领域。它采用了一个求解器框架，可以由多个模型驱动，包括像GPT-5.4这样的强大前沿模型，并且还集成了一个用户模拟器以实现多轮交互。最后，FaraGen1.5使用三个互补的验证器对生成的轨迹进行评分，涵盖任务正确性、效率和关键点遵循。利用该流水线生成的数据，我们训练了Fara1.5，这是一个基于Qwen3.5（4B、9B和27B）构建的三个规模的本地计算机使用智能体（CUA）家族。为了训练这些模型，我们采用了一种监督微调（SFT）方案，该方案仔细平衡了来自FaraGen1.5的数据，以实现广泛覆盖、特定高价值任务，并以迭代方式针对目标模型的缺陷。每个模型在浏览器使用基准测试上都为其规模类别设立了新的最先进水平：Fara1.5-9B在Online-Mind2Web上达到63.4%，在WebVoyager上达到86.6%，而Fara1.5-27B在Online-Mind2Web上达到72.3%，与更大的专有系统相比具有竞争力。

Original abstract: Collecting computer use data from human demonstrations is expensive and slow, motivating the need for scalable generation strategies. This requires two key ingredients: environments in which agents can act and verifiers that can judge whether their demonstrations succeeded. We introduce FaraGen1.5, a scalable data pipeline for computer use agents composed of three modular components: environments, solvers, and verifiers. FaraGen1.5 uses both live websites and synthetic environments that faithfully simulate domains gated by authentication or that require irreversible actions. It employs a solver harness that can be powered by multiple models, including strong frontier models such as GPT-5.4, and also incorporates a user simulator to enable multi-turn rollouts. Finally, FaraGen1.5 scores the resulting trajectories with three complementary verifiers covering task correctness, efficiency, and critical-point adherence. Using data produced by this pipeline, we train Fara1.5, a family of native computer use agents (CUAs) at three scales built on Qwen3.5 (4B, 9B, and 27B). To train these models, we employ a supervised finetuning (SFT) recipe that carefully balances data from FaraGen1.5 for broad coverage, specific high-value tasks, and target model deficiencies in an iterative approach. Each model sets a new state of the art for its size class on browser-use benchmarks: Fara1.5-9B reaches 63.4% on Online-Mind2Web and 86.6% on WebVoyager, while Fara1.5-27B achieves 72.3% on Online-Mind2Web, which is competitive with much larger proprietary systems.

### [59] [Process-Reward Tactic Evolution for Long-Horizon Bioinformatics Workflows](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20839v1)
*Lingzhi Yang,Yubo Fan,Song Wu,Gilchan Park*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出长程agent的流程奖励策略演化训练框架，包含课程环境、验证器和策略库，可迁移到代码优化agent。

TL;DR: 提出了Process-Reward Tactic Evolution框架，通过过程奖励和监督策略积累，提升LLM智能体在长期生物信息学工作流中的执行成功率和生物学正确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前LLM智能体在长期、多步骤的生物信息学工作流执行中表现不佳，需要可靠的交互、类型检查、溯源和生物学验证，现有方法缺乏对过程质量的监督和可重用策略的积累。

Method: 设计基于Galaxy的Agent Gym训练环境，使用过程验证器评估工作流构建、执行和生物学正确性，将成功和失败轨迹蒸馏为策略库；推理时智能体（Process-Reward Tactic Evolution）利用策略库执行新任务。

Result: 在BioWorkflow Bench和BioAgent Bench任务上，Process-Reward Tactic Evolution相比无记忆和反思基线，在长期工作流完成率、生物学正确性和执行效率上表现更优。

Conclusion: 过程监督的策略积累有效提升了LLM智能体在复杂生物信息学工作流中的可靠性和效率，验证了该框架的实用价值。

中文摘要：LLM智能体可以编写代码和调用工具，但可靠的生物信息学工作需要与工作流软件、类型化数据对象、溯源和生物学检查进行长期交互。我们通过Galaxy工作流执行来研究这一场景。智能体必须探索任务数据，构建或调整可执行的工作流有向无环图（DAG），绑定输入和数据集集合，监控执行，调试失败，并验证生物学输出。我们提出了过程奖励策略进化（Process-Reward Tactic Evolution），一个基于Galaxy的训练框架，将经过验证的工作流部署转化为可重用的“策略”。在训练期间，智能体在Agent Gym中练习课程组织的Galaxy任务；过程验证器对工作流构建、软件交互、执行和生物学正确性进行评分；成功和失败的轨迹被提炼到策略库中。在推理时，经过训练的执行器（Process-Reward Tactic Evolution）使用这个库在隔离环境中执行保留的同行评审Galaxy工作流（转换为BioWorkflow Bench和BioAgent Bench任务）。本文评估了过程监督的策略积累是否优于无记忆和反思式基线，在长期生物信息学工作流完成、生物学正确性和执行效率方面。

Original abstract: LLM agents can write code and call tools, but reliable bioinformatics work requires long-horizon interaction with workflow software, typed data objects, provenance, and biological checks. We study this setting through Galaxy workflow execution. The agent must explore task data, construct or adapt an executable workflow DAG, bind inputs and dataset collections, monitor execution, debug failures, and validate biological outputs. We propose Process-Reward Tactic Evolution, a Galaxy-based training framework that turns verified workflow rollouts into reusable \tactics. During training, agents practice on curriculum-organized Galaxy tasks in Agent Gym; process verifiers score workflow construction, software interaction, execution, and biological correctness; successful and failed traces are distilled into a tactic library. At inference, the trained executor, Process-Reward Tactic Evolution, uses this library to execute held-out peer reviewed Galaxy workflow converted BioWorkflow Bench and BioAgent Bench tasks in isolated environments. The paper evaluates whether process-supervised tactic accumulation improves long-horizon bioinformatics workflow completion, biological correctness, and execution efficiency over no-memory and reflection-style baselines.

</details>


### [60] [When Do Intrinsic Rewards Work for Code Reasoning? A Comprehensive Study](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20881v1)
*Xiaolong Jin,Xuandong Zhao,Wenbo Guo,Xiangyu Zhang,Dawn Song*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 研究代码推理任务的强化学习内在奖励方法，直接关联coding agent训练

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了内在奖励方法在代码生成中的应用，发现基于置信度的RLIF方法早期有效但最终崩溃，且RLIF预训练对RLVR无显著提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 代码生成需要可验证奖励，但真实监督昂贵或不可行；内在奖励方法在数学推理中成功，但在代码领域尚未被探索。

Method: 在LiveCodeBench上对基于置信度的内部反馈强化学习（RLIF）方法进行系统实验，评估不同训练场景和超参数。

Result: RLIF方法早期有收益但最终崩溃，输出缩短、推理能力丧失；崩溃速度受样本量和温度影响；RLIF预训练对后续RLVR无显著优势。

Conclusion: 内在奖励方法在代码生成中有潜力但存在局限，提议了使用建议并为未来研究提供指导。

中文摘要：具有可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）推动了大型语言模型推理能力的显著进步，但其依赖于昂贵或不可行的真实监督，尤其是在编程任务中。最近的研究通过从模型自身的信号（如多数投票或基于置信度的得分）中推导奖励来解决这一问题，并在数学推理基准上取得了显著成功。然而，代码生成带来了独特的挑战：程序在结构上复杂，语义上等价的解决方案可能在语法上不同，并且验证通常需要执行。这些内在奖励方法是否能有效迁移到代码领域仍未被探索。在这项工作中，我们对代码生成的内在奖励方法进行了系统的实证研究。我们在LiveCodeBench上进行了大量实验，系统地评估了具有代表性的基于置信度的内部反馈强化学习（RLIF）方法在不同训练场景和超参数设置下的表现。我们的实验表明，基于置信度的方法在早期有收益，但最终不可避免地崩溃：模型逐渐缩短输出并失去推理能力，崩溃速度对样本量和温度敏感。当用于初始化RLVR训练时，RLIF预训练与从头训练相比没有显著改进。我们还为使用内在奖励训练代码推理模型提供了可行的建议。我们的研究显示了内在奖励方法在代码领域的潜力和局限性，为未来代码模型和智能体的研究提供了信息。

Original abstract: Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) has driven substantial progress in large language model reasoning, but relies on ground-truth supervision that is costly or infeasible, especially in coding tasks. Recent work addresses this by deriving rewards from a model's own signals, such as majority voting or confidence-based scores, achieving notable success on mathematical reasoning benchmarks. However, code generation poses distinct challenges: programs are structurally complex, semantically equivalent solutions may differ syntactically, and verification typically requires execution. Whether these intrinsic reward methods transfer effectively to code remains unexplored. In this work, we present a systematic empirical study of intrinsic reward methods for code generation. We conduct extensive experiments on LiveCodeBench, systematically evaluating representative certainty-based Reinforcement Learning from Internal Feedback (RLIF) approaches under different training scenarios and hyperparameter settings. Our experiments reveal that certainty-based methods yield early gains but inevitably collapse: models progressively shorten outputs and lose reasoning capability, with collapse speed sensitive to sample size and temperature. When used to initialize RLVR training, RLIF pre-training offers no significant improvement over training from scratch. We also provide actionable recommendations for using intrinsic rewards for training code reasoning models. Our study shows both the promise and limitations of intrinsic reward methods for code, informing future work on code models and agents.

</details>


### [61] [Power Systems Agent Benchmark: Executable Evaluation of AI Agents in Electric Power Engineering](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20950v2)
*Sergei Trashchenkov*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 电力系统agent可执行基准，通用agent评估方法

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个面向电力工程智能体的可执行基准，包含41个任务族，覆盖八个领域，采用确定性评估和抗污染保留案例。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 电力工程领域缺乏针对AI智能体的可执行基准，现有语言模型应用局限于检索和问答，该基准填补了这一空白。

Method: 构建了结构化任务与确定性评估器，检查工程约束；包含41个任务族来自八个领域，通过私有种子按需生成保留案例以避免数据污染。

Result: 参考评估中，最强智能体分数接近上限，较小开放模型表现落后，公开与保留性能一致；评估还作为质量控制，发现了一个潜在评估器错误。

Conclusion: 该基准提供了鲁棒且可扩展的电力工程AI智能体评估方法，具备确定性评分和可升级的评估器。

中文摘要：可执行评估——通过程序检查智能体行动的后果，而非对其文本输出进行评分——已成为评估软件环境中使用工具的AI智能体的重要方法。电力工程领域尚未有类似的基准：语言模型的使用仍以检索和文本问答为主，而对电力系统工件进行操作的智能体大多停留在学术原型阶段。我们介绍了电力系统智能体基准（Power Systems Agent Benchmark），这是一个面向电力工程智能体的可执行基准。智能体接收结构化任务并返回结构化解决方案；确定性评估器重新计算工程量，检查运行约束，并返回可行性标志、归一化分数和显式违规信息。该基准包含41个任务族，涵盖电力工程的八个领域，从潮流和保护到稳定性、微电网、可靠性、电能质量和预测。每个任务都基于可引用来源、标准或已记录的工程公式。为了抵抗数据污染，通过每个任务族的私有种子按需合成保留案例：构造是可审查的，但实例保持私有。在三个命令行智能体的参考评估中，最强的分数接近紧凑层的上限，较小的开放模型落后，公开和保留的性能大体一致；一个单独的公开分割网格与OpenCode和Aider探测了助手的效应。参考评估同时作为质量控制：一致失败标记候选任务或评估器的缺陷，并暴露了一个被自一致性检查遗漏的潜在评估器错误。评估器是紧凑的确定性替代品，但任务契约允许其内部升级为模拟器支持的检查，而无需改变任务的提出或解决方式。

Original abstract: Executable evaluation -- checking the consequences of an agent's actions with a program rather than grading its prose -- has become a prominent way to assess tool-using AI agents in software settings. Electric power engineering has not yet had an analogous benchmark: language-model use is still dominated by retrieval and text question answering, while agents acting on power-system artifacts remain mostly academic prototypes. We introduce the Power Systems Agent Benchmark, an executable benchmark for power-engineering agents. An agent receives a structured task and returns a structured solution; a deterministic evaluator recomputes the engineering quantities, checks operational constraints, and returns a feasibility flag, a normalized score, and explicit violations.
  The benchmark contains 41 task families across eight areas of power engineering, from power flow and protection to stability, microgrids, reliability, power quality, and forecasting. Each task is grounded in a citable source, standard, or documented engineering formulation. To resist contamination, held-out cases are synthesized on demand by per-family generators from private seeds: the construction is inspectable, but the instances remain private. In a reference evaluation with three command-line agents, the strongest score near the compact tier's ceiling, a smaller open model trails, and public and held-out performance are broadly consistent; a separate public-split grid with OpenCode and Aider probes harness effects. The reference evaluation doubles as quality control: unanimous failures flag candidate task or evaluator defects, and it exposed a latent evaluator bug missed by self-consistency checks. The evaluators are compact deterministic surrogates, but the task contract allows their internals to be upgraded to simulator-backed checks without changing how tasks are posed or solved.

### [62] [AutoACSL: Synthesizing ACSL Specifications by Integrating LLMs with CPG-Based Static Analysis](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20969v1)
*Han Zhou,Yu Luo,Dianxiang Xu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出AutoACSL框架，结合LLM和代码属性图静态分析，实现高成功率的自动化ACSL规约生成与验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前自动规约合成方法缺乏语义深度，产生不可验证或不完整的契约，亟需一种融合语义特征和迭代验证的框架。

Method: AutoACSL从代码属性图提取算术运算、循环/递归结构、返回值传播等语义特征，编码为结构化提示引导LLM生成含约束规约，并通过Frama-C/WP进行反馈驱动的迭代验证与精炼。

Result: 在604个程序上，与Gemini-3配对时规约生成成功率98%，完整证明率96%；相比仅代码基线，四个LLM的完整证明率提升24.7%-51.7%。

Conclusion: 将LLM与基于CPG的静态分析相结合显著增强了自动化ACSL规约合成的生成鲁棒性和验证有效性。

中文摘要：为C程序生成形式规约仍然是形式验证中的一个挑战，因为这需要大量的人工努力、专业知识和语义精度。尽管近期大型语言模型（LLM）的进展为自动化规约合成带来了希望，但当前的方法通常缺乏语义深度，并产生不可验证或不完整的契约。为了解决这些局限性，我们引入了AutoACSL，这是一个新颖的框架，它将LLM提示与从代码属性图（CPG）中提取的语义特征相结合。AutoACSL执行静态分析以提取关键的语义元素，包括算术运算、循环和递归结构以及返回值传播，这些元素被编码到结构化提示中。这些提示使LLM不仅能够生成正常行为规约，还能包含防止导致运行时错误的输入的约束。AutoACSL采用反馈驱动的合成循环，其中候选规约使用Frama-C/WP进行验证，并迭代精炼，直到验证成功或满足终止条件。在来自不同数据集的604个程序上评估，AutoACSL与Gemini-3配对时实现了98%的规约生成成功率和96%的完整证明率。与仅代码基线相比，AutoACSL在四个LLM（GPT-o4 Mini、GPT-5.2、Grok-4.1和Gemini-3）上将完整证明率提高了24.7%到51.7%，这表明将大型语言模型与基于CPG的静态分析相结合显著增强了自动化ACSL规约合成的生成鲁棒性和验证有效性。

Original abstract: Generating formal specifications for C programs remains a challenge in formal verification due to the manual effort, expertise, and semantic precision required. While recent advancements in large language models (LLMs) offer promise in automating specification synthesis, current approaches often lack semantic depth and produce unverifiable or incomplete contracts. To address these limitations, we introduce AutoACSL, a novel framework that integrates LLM prompting with semantic features extracted from Code Property Graphs (CPGs). AutoACSL performs static analyses to extract key semantic elements, including arithmetic operations, loop and recursion structures, and return value propagation, which are encoded into structured prompts. These prompts enable the LLM not only to generate normal behavioral specifications but also to include constraints that prevent inputs leading to runtime errors. AutoACSL employs a feedback-driven synthesis loop, where candidate specifications are verified using Frama-C/WP and refined iteratively until verification succeeds or a termination condition is met. Evaluated on 604 programs drawn from diverse datasets, AutoACSL achieves a 98% specification generation success ratio and a 96% full proof ratio when paired with Gemini-3. Compared to a code-only baseline, AutoACSL improves the full proof ratio by 24.7% to 51.7% across four LLMs (GPT-o4 Mini, GPT-5.2, Grok-4.1, and Gemini-3), demonstrating that integrating large language models with CPG-based static analysis substantially enhances both generation robustness and verification effectiveness for automated ACSL specification synthesis.

</details>


### [63] [How Should Agents Read Demonstrations? Hierarchical Structure Beats Flat Action Logs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20978v1)
*Honjar Xing,Jefferson Lin,Henry Lieberman*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 研究演示层次结构对LLM agent规划效果的影响，方法可迁移至coding agent。

TL;DR: 本文研究按示例编程中演示格式的组织结构对LLM代理任务性能的影响，发现将动作日志分组为分层子目标能显著提高模糊描述任务的通过率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: PbD产生的扁平动作日志如何组织影响计划质量，但该设计问题尚未解决，因此探索更好的组织结构。

Method: 提出将记录动作分组为带标签的分层子目标，在85个Web自动化任务上比较零样本基线及四种结构化格式（扁平、分层等），并对43个模糊描述和42个精确描述任务分别评估。

Result: 分层分组在模糊描述任务中通过率从76.7%提升至90.7%（p=0.034），而扁平格式无显著提升；精确描述任务中所有格式均无改善；消融表明仅子目标分组起作用。

Conclusion: 建议PbD系统将动作序列分割为命名的子目标组，而非呈现扁平步骤列表，以提升LLM代理在模糊任务中的表现。

中文摘要：按示例编程（PbD）提供了一种以人为中心的方式，为LLM代理编写程序性知识：用户通过展示而非编写提示或代码来传达他们的需求，使得非程序员也能进行代理编写。PbD记录的自然输出是一个扁平的动作日志，但在将日志传递给代理之前如何组织它，是一个开放的设计问题，对计划质量有重大影响。我们提出将记录的动作分组为带有标签的分层子目标，并在受控实验中评估这种组织结构的影响。在85个Web自动化任务中，我们比较了一个零样本基线以及四种演示格式，这些格式具有相同的动作序列但结构不同。在43个具有模糊描述的自然语言任务中，分层分组的演示将通过率从76.7%提高到90.7%（配对置换检验p=0.034；胜率6:0），而扁平演示则显示出更小且不显著的改进。在42个具有精确描述的任务中，没有一种格式提供了任何好处，证实了分层优势仅在描述留下程序细节模糊时才出现。消融实验表明，子目标分组单独驱动了效果：前置条件、后置条件和参数注释没有增加可衡量的好处。这些结果为PbD流程以及更广泛地，为任何向LLM代理提供程序性上下文的系统提供了一个具体的设计建议：将动作序列分割成命名的子目标组，而不是呈现扁平的步骤列表。

Original abstract: Programming by Demonstration (PbD) offers a human-centered way to author procedural knowledge for LLM agents: users communicate what they want by showing rather than by writing prompts or code, making agent authoring accessible to non-programmers. The natural output of a PbD recording is a flat action log, but how this log is organized before being passed to the agent is an open design question with significant consequences for plan quality. We propose grouping recorded actions into labeled, hierarchical subgoals and evaluate the effect of this organizational structure in a controlled experiment. Across 85 web automation tasks, we compare a zero-shot baseline against four demonstration formats that share identical action sequences but differ in structure. On 43 natural-language tasks with vague descriptions, hierarchically grouped demonstrations improve pass rates from 76.7\% to 90.7\% (paired permutation test $p{=}0.034$; win-loss 6:0), while flat demonstrations show a smaller, non-significant improvement. On 42 tasks with precise descriptions, no format provides any benefit, confirming that the hierarchical advantage arises specifically when descriptions leave procedural details ambiguous. Ablation shows that subgoal grouping alone drives the effect: preconditions, postconditions, and parameter annotations add no measurable benefit. These results offer a concrete design recommendation for PbD pipelines and, more broadly, for any system that feeds procedural context to an LLM agent: segment action sequences into named subgoal groups rather than presenting flat step lists.

</details>
