### [64] [Large Language Models Do Not Always Need Readable Language](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19857v1)
*Jiayi Zhu,Haoxuan Peng,Junxi Wang,Liang Ke,Chen Zhang,Linfeng Zhang*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 研究LLM非可读文本表示，涉及agent记忆和多agent通信，属通用agent方法

TL;DR: 本文提出BabelTele，一种紧凑的非人类可读文本表示，能在大幅压缩文本至27.9%长度时保持99.5%语义保真度，并验证了其在指令调优LLM中的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM交互依赖人类可读自然语言，导致上下文冗余，需要探索更高效的模型间通信表示，以降低开销并保持语义。

Method: 通过可读性诊断、模型似然度量、人类问卷和下游任务评估BabelTele的性能；进一步在跨模型迁移、代理记忆和多代理通信中测试其语义鲁棒性。

Result: BabelTele在压缩至27.9%长度时保持99.5%语义保真度；在跨模型迁移、代理记忆和多代理通信中通常保持可靠性能，但效果依赖于压缩器-读取器对和任务设置。

Conclusion: 人类可读性、自然语言典型性和模型侧语义可恢复性可以部分解耦，BabelTele为模型原生表示提供了可行方向。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLMs）通常以人类可读的自然语言进行提示和交互，即使预期读者是另一个模型。本文研究是否可以将语义信息编码为紧凑的、非标准的文本形式，这种形式牺牲了人类可读性，但仍能被LLMs恢复。我们将这类以模型为中心的文本表示称为BabelTele，这里不是作为一种固定协议，而是作为对LLMs生成和解释这类表示能力的经验性探究。通过可读性诊断、模型似然度量、人类问卷和下游任务评估，我们发现BabelTele可以大幅偏离普通自然语言，同时为指令调优的LLMs保留核心语义。作为一种任务无关的表示范式，BabelTele展示了高信息密度，即使在文本体积压缩到原始长度的27.9%时，仍保持99.5%的语义保真度。我们进一步评估了其在跨模型迁移、代理记忆和多代理通信中的语义鲁棒性。结果表明，BabelTele可以减少上下文开销，同时通常保持可靠的下游性能，尽管其有效性取决于压缩器-读取器对和任务设置。这些发现表明，人类可读性、自然语言典型性和模型侧语义可恢复性可以部分解耦，为未来探索LLM系统中面向模型的表示开辟了一条道路。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are commonly prompted and interfaced with human-readable natural language, even when the intended reader is another model. This paper investigates whether semantic information can be encoded in compact, non-standard textual forms that sacrifice human readability while remaining recoverable by LLMs. We refer to this class of model-centric textual representations as BabelTele, approached here not as a fixed protocol but as an empirical probe into LLMs' capacity to generate and interpret such representations. Through readability diagnostics, model likelihood measures, human questionnaires, and downstream task evaluations, we find that BabelTele can substantially depart from ordinary natural language while preserving core semantics for instruction-tuned LLMs. As a task-agnostic representational paradigm, BabelTele demonstrates high information density, maintaining 99.5% semantic fidelity even when the text volume is condensed to 27.9% of its original length. We further evaluate its semantic robustness in cross-model transfer, agent memory, and multi-agent communication. Results suggest that BabelTele can reduce context overhead while generally maintaining reliable downstream performance, although its effectiveness depends on the compressor-reader pair and task setting. These findings indicate that human readability, natural-language typicality, and model-side semantic recoverability can be partially decoupled, opening a path toward model-native representations in future exploration of LLM systems.

</details>


### [65] [Latent Personal Memory: Represent personal memory as dynamic soft prompts](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20911v1)
*Debrup Das,Avinash Amballa,Yashas Malur Saidutta,Vijay Srinivasan,Vivek Kulkarni,Srinivas Chappidi*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 潜在记忆表示方法，适用于agent长期记忆管理

TL;DR: 提出潜在个人记忆（LPM），通过可解释的潜在槽和交叉注意力投影生成软提示，实现高效个性化LLM，在准确率和计算效率上显著优于LoRA和Prompt Tuning。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有个性化LLM方法（如LoRA、Prompt Tuning）在编码长期用户行为模式时存在计算效率低、参数开销大或与冻结模型不兼容的问题，需要一种更高效且可扩展的框架。

Method: LPM将用户历史编码为N个可解释的潜在槽矩阵，通过共享交叉注意力投影网络生成输入条件的软提示，预置到冻结LLM的输入中。

Result: 在PersonaMem v1上，LPM准确率比LoRA高8.8%、比Prompt Tuning高54.4%，KV缓存减少64倍；在LoCoMo上以120倍更少参数匹配LoRA准确率；在128K上下文长度下优于全上下文。

Conclusion: LPM是一种高效、可扩展且与冻结LLM兼容的个性化框架，在准确率和资源效率上均优于现有方法，且受益于长上下文。

中文摘要：个性化大型语言模型（LLMs）需要以计算高效、可扩展且与冻结的基础模型兼容的方式编码长期、用户特定的行为模式。我们提出了潜在个人记忆（LPM），这是一个可扩展的框架，将用户特定的历史表示为紧凑、持久的N个潜在槽矩阵，这些槽是可解释的。一个共享的交叉注意力投影网络将这些槽映射为动态的、输入条件的软提示，这些提示被预置到冻结LLM的输入之前。我们在PersonaMem v1和LoCOMO基准上使用Qwen3-1.7B、4B和8B骨干网络评估LPM。结果表明，LPM在PersonaMem v1上的整体准确率分别比LoRA和Prompt Tuning高出高达8.8%和54.4%，同时KV缓存使用减少超过64倍。在LoCoMo上，LPM以120倍更少的可训练参数匹配了LoRA的准确率。我们还展示了LPM的效率随上下文长度增长，并在128K上下文长度上优于全上下文。

Original abstract: Personalizing large language models (LLMs) requires encoding long-term, user-specific behavioral patterns in a way that is computationally efficient, scalable, and compatible with a frozen base model. We present Latent Personal Memory (LPM), a scalable framework that represents user-specific history as a compact, persistent matrix of N latent slots, that are interpretable. A shared cross-attention projection network maps these slots into dynamic, input-conditioned soft prompts that are prepended to the input of a frozen LLM. We evaluate LPM on PersonaMem v1 and LoCOMO benchmarks across Qwen3-1.7B, 4B, and 8B backbones. Results demonstrate that LPM outperforms LoRA and Prompt Tuning by up to 8.8% and 54.4% in overall accuracy respectively on PersonaMem v1, while reducing KV-cache usage by over 64x. On LoCoMo, LPM matches LoRA accuracy with 120x fewer trainable parameters. We also show that the efficiency of LPM grows with context length and outperforms full-context at 128K context length.

</details>


### [66] [Learning What Not to Forget: Long-Horizon Agent Memory from a Few Kilobytes of Learning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20954v1)
*Nusrat Jahan Lia,Aritra Mazumder*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 长程agent记忆逐出策略，直接关系agent记忆与任务完成

TL;DR: LRE是一种轻量级的学习相关性驱逐策略，用于LLM长上下文管理，在多项任务上优于基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有驱逐策略丢弃关键细节导致任务失败，需要廉价有效的主动驱逐策略。

Method: 提出LRE，一个几KB大小、仅CPU运行的无语言模型评分器，学习关键历史单元并通过逐字提取保留。

Result: LRE在准确性-成本平面上优于所有基线；在智能体任务上匹配完整历史准确性，简单任务提升27%，减少52%上下文大小；完成其他策略无法完成的任务；在对话记忆中零神经成本超越其他编码器；LoCoMo上阅读减少68%令牌达到最佳质量；无标注训练恢复95%效果。

Conclusion: LLM内存驱逐是保真度问题，需主动策略，廉价学习相关性足够有效。

中文摘要：长时间运行的语言模型系统会积累超出上下文窗口的交互历史，因此必须持续进行驱逐。当驱逐策略丢弃一个关键细节（例如登录时颁发的访问令牌或下一次调用所需的路径）时，操作会失败。我们提出了LRE（学习相关性驱逐），一个仅几KB、仅CPU、无语言模型的评分器，它学习哪些历史单元是关键性的，并通过逐字提取保留它们。在匹配预算的比较下，在我们的实验中，没有基线的准确性-成本曲线能优于LRE。在智能体上，LRE总体上匹配了保留整个历史的准确性。在最简单的任务上，它比无驱逐基线提高了27%，同时不需要任何压缩器调用，并将峰值上下文大小减少了高达52%。一项受控研究追踪显示，LRE完成了其他策略陷入循环的任务，其中一个任务在比保留全部历史少37%的调用次数内完成，并解决了14个其他运行策略无法完成的任务。在对话记忆中，LRE以零神经成本超越了密集和令牌剪枝编码器。在下游评估中，LRE在LoCoMo上以读取减少68%的令牌取得了最佳预算答案质量。它的监督也可以是无标注的：仅基于系统自身行为进行训练就能恢复有监督评分器95%的效果。我们认为，由于LLM智能体中的内存驱逐是一个保真度问题，它需要一个可部署的主动策略，其中未来查询不可用且确切状态是关键，而廉价的学习相关性可能就足够了。

Original abstract: Long-running language-model systems accumulate interaction history that outgrows the context window, so they must continually evict. When an eviction policy drops a load-bearing detail, for example an access token issued at login or a path the next call needs, the action fails. We present LRE (Learned Relevance Eviction), a few kilobytes, CPU-only, language-model-free scorer that learns which units of history are load-bearing and keeps them by verbatim extraction. Under a matched-budget comparison, in our experiment, no baseline dominates LRE on the accuracy-cost plane. On agents, LRE matches the accuracy of keeping the entire history overall. On the simplest tasks, it exceeds that no-eviction baseline by 27%, while requiring zero compressor calls and reducing peak context size by up to 52%. A controlled study trace shows LRE completes tasks where the others loop, finishing one such task in 37% fewer calls than keeping everything and solving 14 tasks where no other run policy does. On conversational memory, LRE outranks dense and token-pruning encoders at zero neural cost. In downstream evaluation, LRE gives the best budgeted answer quality on LoCoMo reading 68% fewer tokens. Its supervision can also be annotation-free: training only on the system's own behavior recovers 95% of the supervised scorer's effectiveness. We argue that, because memory eviction in LLM agents is a fidelity problem, it requires a deployable proactive policy where the future query is unavailable and exact state is decisive, and that cheap learned relevance can be sufficient.

</details>

### [67] [Measuring Biological Capabilities and Risks of AI Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19899v1)
*Patricia Paskov,Jeffrey Lee,Kyle Brady,Alyssa Worland*

Main category: cs.CY

Selection reason: AI agent生物能力与风险评估，涉及agent评测和安全

TL;DR: 本文提出生物智能体评估是评估AI生物风险的关键工具，但结果解读高度依赖评估设计选择，并提供了经验性指导帮助决策者正确解读。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AI科学家系统进入研究流程，但评估结果的含义常因设计选择不透明而难以解读，迫切需要可信证据生成与解释方法。

Method: 综合当前AI生物风险证据，引入生物智能体评估概念，并根据自身评估经验总结定义、设计、运行、评分、文档化等环节的设计选择对结果含义的影响。

Result: 评估选择（如定义、设计、运行、评分、文档）会实质性地改变结果对风险的含义。

Conclusion: 本分析帮助政策制定者谨慎解读评估结果，引导投资者聚焦高效领域，并支持生物安全从业者，同时服务于评估设计研究人员。

中文摘要：本文探讨了一个迅速出现的政策挑战：如何生成和解释关于AI科学家（即能够自主或协作执行多步科学任务的智能体AI系统）的生物能力与风险的可信证据。随着这些系统进入真实的研究工作流程，决策者越来越多地面临评估结果，而这些结果的含义取决于通常隐含或未充分记录的基础设计选择。我们综合了当前关于AI引发的生物风险的证据，并引入了生物智能体评估作为一种有前景但依赖解释的工具来评估这些系统。我们的核心贡献是一套基于经验的实际考虑——源自我们自身的评估——展示了关于定义、设计、运行、评分和记录评估的选择如何实质性地影响结果对风险的含义。该分析旨在帮助政策制定者以适当的谨慎态度解释生物评估输出；指导公共和私人资助者向AI-生物学评估研究中的高杠杆投资；并支持评估新兴AI系统的生物安全从业者。次要受众包括在前沿AI实验室、AI提供商、科学机构和第三方评估组织内设计或进行智能体评估的研究人员。

Original abstract: This paper addresses a rapidly emerging policy challenge: how to generate and interpret credible evidence about the biological capabilities and risks of AI scientists, or agentic AI systems capable of autonomously or collaboratively performing multi-step scientific tasks. As these systems enter real research workflows, decision-makers increasingly face evaluation results whose meaning depends on underlying design choices that are often implicit or under-documented. We synthesize current evidence on AI-enabled biological risks and introduce biological agentic evaluations as a promising, but interpretation-sensitive, tool for assessing these systems. Our central contribution is a set of practical, experience-grounded considerations -- drawing from our own evaluations -- that show how choices around defining, designing, running, scoring, and documenting evaluations materially shape what results do and do not imply about risk. The analysis is intended to help policymakers interpret biological evaluation outputs with appropriate caution; guide public and private funders toward high-leverage investments in AI-biology evaluation research; and support biosecurity practitioners assessing emerging AI systems. A secondary audience includes researchers designing or conducting agentic evaluations within frontier AI labs, AI providers, scientific institutions, and third-party evaluation organizations.

### [68] [Efficiently Representing Algorithms With Chain-of-Thought Transformers](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19697v1)
*Yanhong Li,Anej Svete,Ashish Sabharwal,William Merrill*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: CoT Transformer模拟算法推理，对agent推理机制有启发。

TL;DR: 本文证明思维链Transformer可以高效模拟Word RAM算法，仅增加多对数开销，并在三种架构下验证了这一点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 图灵机模型对于算法讨论不高效，而Word RAM模型更符合实际算法设计，因此探究CoT Transformer能否高效模拟Word RAM算法。

Method: 先针对具有多对数宽度和最右唯一硬注意力的有限精度Transformer建立模拟，再扩展到有限宽度和对数精度的连续CoT以及混合架构（RNN+Transformer）。

Result: 三种架构下，CoT Transformer可以模拟任何Word RAM算法，仅有多对数开销；扁平指令集下开销降至对数平方，无乘法扁平指令下仅为对数。

Conclusion: CoT Transformer能够高效模拟实际算法，相比图灵机模拟有显著改进（平方开销降至多对数）。

中文摘要：推理模型的日益流行——语言模型在给出答案之前输出一系列推理或思考token——部分由理论结果所证明，这些结果表明思维链（CoT）Transformer可以模拟图灵机，从而执行任意计算。然而，图灵机虽然适合复杂性理论分析，但对于讨论算法而言并不方便、直观或高效。算法通常是在更高的抽象层次上设计和分析的，由具有随机访问存储器和$\bigO(\log n)$位字的单位成本操作的Word RAM模型体现。因此，Word RAM算法可能比其图灵机对应物高效得多，这引发了一个问题：CoT Transformer能否高效模拟Word RAM算法？例如，它们能否在$\bigO(n \log n)$步内对n个元素进行排序，或在$\bigO(E + V \log V)$步内运行Dijkstra算法？我们给出了肯定的回答，且只增加多对数开销。我们首先针对具有多对数宽度和最右唯一硬注意力的有限精度Transformer建立了这一结果，然后将结果推广到两种更实际的设置：有限宽度和对数精度的连续CoT（其中推理采用向量而非token的形式）以及混合架构（其中Transformer层位于循环（线性RNN）层之上）。在所有三种情况下，我们发现CoT确实可以高效模拟任何Word RAM算法，且仅增加$n$的多对数开销。当Word RAM具有“扁平”指令集时，此开销降至对数平方，对于无乘法扁平指令则仅需对数开销——这与已知的CoT模拟图灵机（需要平方开销）形成鲜明对比。

Original abstract: The increasing popularity of \emph{reasoning} models -- language models that output a series of reasoning or thought tokens before producing an answer -- is justified, in part, by theoretical results showing that chain-of-thought (CoT) transformers can simulate Turing machines, and thus perform arbitrary computation. However, the Turing machine, while suitable for complexity-theoretic analysis, is not convenient, intuitive, or efficient for discussing algorithms. Algorithms are typically designed and analyzed at a higher level of abstraction, captured by the \emph{Word RAM} model with random-access memory and unit-cost operations on $\bigO(\log n)$-bit words. As a result, Word RAM algorithms can be substantially more efficient than their Turing machine counterparts, raising the question: \emph{Can CoT transformers efficiently simulate Word RAM algorithms?} For instance, can they sort $n$ items in $\bigO(n \log n)$ steps or run Dijkstra's algorithm in $\bigO(E + V \log V)$ steps? We answer affirmatively, up to poly-logarithmic overhead. We first establish this for finite-precision transformers with poly-logarithmic width and rightmost unique hard attention, then strengthen the result to two more practical settings with finite width and log-precision: \emph{continuous} CoT, where reasoning takes the form of vectors rather than tokens, and a \emph{hybrid} architecture in which transformer layers sit atop a recurrent (linear RNN) layer. In all three cases, we find that CoT \emph{can} efficiently simulate any Word RAM algorithm with only a poly-logarithmic overhead in $n$. This overhead reduces to log-square when the Word RAM has a ``flat'' instruction set, and only logarithmic for multiplication-free flat instructions -- in stark contrast to known CoT simulations of Turing machines, which require quadratic overhead over Word RAM.

</details>


### [69] [Connect the Dots: Training LLMs for Long-Lifecycle Agents with Cross-Domain Generalization Via Reinforcement Learning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20002v1)
*Yanxi Chen,Weijie Shi,Yuexiang Xie,Boyi Hu,Yaliang Li,Bolin Ding,Jingren Zhou*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 训练LLM长期agent框架，使用RL实现跨域泛化，高度相关。

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为“连接点”（CoD）的通用框架，通过端到端强化学习训练LLM具备长生命周期智能体的元能力，并在多个环境中验证了其泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长生命周期智能体需要连续探索和学习的能力，但现有方法难以有效训练LLM具备这种元能力。

Method: 采用GRPO风格的RL算法，设计交织求解任务和更新上下文的长序列，以及定制任务和环境。

Result: 验证了端到端RL训练的有效性，展示了域内、跨域和到Ralph-loop的分布外泛化。

Conclusion: 连接了先前工作，为LLM和AI智能体研究开辟新机会，并开源实现。

中文摘要：本文提出了一个通用框架，用于训练大型语言模型（LLMs）具备“连接点”（CoD）能力，这是长生命周期智能体所需的一种元能力：当基于LLM的AI智能体部署到环境中时，它需要解决一系列长期任务，同时持续探索环境、从自身经验中学习，并迭代地自我更新关于环境的上下文，从而在更新后的上下文条件下，在未来任务上逐步取得更好的性能。CoD框架的主要组成部分包括：（1）用于端到端强化学习（RL）的算法设计和基础设施，其中包括交织求解任务和更新上下文情节的长卷展序列；（2）用于在训练过程中激励和激发LLMs中目标元能力的任务和环境，以及在评估过程中忠实衡量进展的任务和环境。我们展示了CoD框架的概念验证实现，包括一种具有细粒度信用分配的GRPO风格RL算法，以及针对目标元能力（而非领域特定LLM能力或标准的逐任务RL）定制的任务和环境。实证结果验证了端到端RL训练在CoD环境中的有效性，并展示了所激发的元能力在训练域内、跨不同域以及从CoD到Ralph-loop环境中的分布外泛化潜力。我们对CoD的研究连接了之前的若干工作，并为推进LLMs和AI智能体开辟了新的机会。为了促进进一步的研究和应用，我们在以下网址发布了我们的实现：\url{https://github.com/agentscope-ai/Trinity-RFT/tree/research/cod/examples/research_cod}。

Original abstract: This work presents a general framework for training large language models (LLMs) to "Connect the Dots" (CoD), a meta-capability required by long-lifecycle agents: as an LLM-based AI agent gets deployed in an environment, it solves a long sequence of tasks while continuously exploring the environment, learning from its own experiences, and iteratively self-updating its context about the environment, thereby achieving progressively better performance on future tasks conditioned on the updated context. Major components of the CoD framework include: (1) algorithm design and infrastructure for end-to-end reinforcement learning (RL) with long rollout sequences interleaving solve-task and update-context episodes; (2) tasks and environments for incentivizing and eliciting the targeted meta-capability in LLMs during training, as well as for faithfully measuring progress during evaluation. We present proof-of-concept implementations of the CoD framework, including a GRPO-style RL algorithm with fine-grained credit assignment, as well as tasks and environments tailored to the targeted meta-capability (rather than domain-specific LLM capabilities or standard task-by-task RL). Empirical results validate the efficacy of end-to-end RL training in the CoD setting, and demonstrate the potential for out-of-distribution generalization -- within the training domains, across different domains, and from CoD to Ralph-loop settings -- of the elicited meta-capability. Our investigation of CoD connects several lines of prior works, and opens up new opportunities for advancing LLMs and AI agents. To facilitate further research and applications, we release our implementations at \url{https://github.com/agentscope-ai/Trinity-RFT/tree/research/cod/examples/research_cod}.

### [70] [Hierarchical Control in Multi-Agent Games: LLM-based Planning and RL Execution](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20014v3)
*Jannik Hösch,Alessandro Sestini,Florian Fuchs,Amir Baghi,Joakim Bergdahl,Iolanda Leite,Konrad Tollmar,Jean-Philippe Barrette-LaPierre,Linus Gisslén*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: LLM规划+RL执行的层次化多agent架构，可迁移。

TL;DR: 使用LLM作为高层控制器选择RL技能，在2v2环境中表现接近手工BT，且更似人类。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决多智能体强化学习中的稀疏奖励、大状态-动作空间和学习协调策略的困难。

Method: 层次化架构，预训练LLM作为集中式策略控制器选择专门RL技能策略，RL策略处理反应式低级执行。

Result: 在2v2 King of the Hill环境中，LLM+RL胜率46.4%，与BT的51.5%统计无显著差异（p=0.103），两者均显著优于Flat RL；用户研究中60%认为LLM+RL最像人类（p=0.027）。

Conclusion: 预训练LLM推理可有效编排预训练RL技能，实现竞争性多智能体协调和优越的感知可信度，无需手动规则工程。

中文摘要：强化学习（RL）在序列决策中取得了强性能，但扩展到复杂多智能体环境仍然具有挑战性，因为奖励稀疏、状态-动作空间大以及学习协调策略的困难。我们提出一种层次化架构，其中预训练的大语言模型（LLM）作为集中式策略控制器，为一组智能体选择专门的RL技能策略，而RL策略处理反应式低级执行。我们在竞争性2v2 King of the Hill环境中评估该混合系统，与行为树（BT）和“扁平”RL（无技能分解的端到端训练）基线进行比较。LLM+RL系统实现了与手工设计BT统计上相当的任务性能（胜率46.4%对51.5%，p=0.103），而两者都显著优于无技能分解训练的Flat RL。一项用户研究（n=15）显示，60%的参与者认为LLM+RL智能体最像人类（p=0.027），理由是行为适应性和战术变异性。这些结果表明，预训练LLM推理可以有效地编排预训练RL技能，实现竞争性多智能体协调和优越的感知可信度，无需手动规则工程。

Original abstract: Reinforcement learning (RL) has achieved strong performance in sequential decision-making, yet scaling to complex multi-agent environments remains challenging due to sparse rewards, large state-action spaces, and the difficulty of learning coordinated strategies. We propose a hierarchical architecture where a pretrained large language model (LLM) acts as a centralized strategic controller that selects among specialized RL skill policies for a team of agents, while RL policies handle reactive low-level execution. We evaluate this hybrid system in a competitive 2v2 King of the Hill environment against behavior tree (BT) and \emph{``Flat''} RL (end-to-end training without skill decomposition) baselines. The LLM+RL system achieves task performance statistically equivalent to hand-crafted BT (46.4\% vs 51.5\% win rate, $p=0.103$) while both significantly outperform Flat RL trained without skill decomposition. A user study ($n=15$) reveals that 60\% of participants perceive LLM+RL agents as the most human-like ($p=0.027$), citing behavioral adaptability and tactical variability. These results demonstrate that pretrained LLM reasoning can effectively orchestrate pretrained RL skills, achieving competitive multi-agent coordination and superior perceived believability without manual rule engineering.

</details>


### [71] [Sensorimotor World Models: Perception for Action via Inverse Dynamics](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20104v1)
*Petr Ivashkov,Randall Balestriero,Bernhard Schölkopf*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 提出传感器运动世界模型，通过逆动力学正则化学习行动对齐表示，对agent中的世界建模和规划有潜在启发。

TL;DR: 提出传感器运动世界模型（SMWM），通过逆动力学正则化端到端训练，同时防止表征坍缩并学习行动对齐的表征，在离线无奖励轨迹上训练，取得紧凑可解释的潜在空间和良好规划性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: JEPA风格世界模型端到端训练时表征容易坍缩，且缺乏与行动的对齐，需要一种既能防止坍缩又能学习行动相关表征的方法。

Method: 提出SMWM，采用逆动力学正则化，迫使潜在状态保留过渡中的行动信息，从而偏向可控自由度，丢弃不可控干扰。

Result: SMWM学到紧凑、可解释的潜在空间，在2D和3D控制任务上规划性能有竞争力，且无需冻结编码器或复杂正则化。

Conclusion: 逆动力学正则化有效解决表征坍缩和行动对齐问题，使得离线无奖励训练稳定，性能良好。

中文摘要：感知用于行动表明，世界的表征不仅应由视觉保真度塑造，还应由其与行动的相关性塑造。同时，潜在的JEPA风格世界模型提倡从高维观测中学习紧凑的预测状态以促进未来状态的预测，但这些模型的端到端训练并非易事，因为如果我们唯一目标是构建易于预测的潜在状态，表征可能会坍缩。我们引入了传感器运动世界模型（SMWM）：一种通过逆动力学正则化进行端到端训练的潜在世界模型。这个单一的正则化解决了两个问题：防止表征坍缩并诱导与行动对齐的表征。通过迫使潜在状态保留关于过渡背后行动的信息，它使模型偏向于环境中可控的自由度，同时丢弃不可控的干扰因素。这产生了稳定的潜在世界模型，可以从离线的、无奖励的轨迹中训练，无需冻结编码器、指数移动平均或复杂的潜在正则化。实验上，SMWM学习了紧凑、可解释的潜在空间，并在简单的2D和3D控制任务中实现了有竞争力的规划性能。

Original abstract: Perception for action suggests that representations of the world should be shaped not by visual fidelity alone, but by their relevance for actions. At the same time, latent JEPA-style world models advocate learning compact predictive states from high-dimensional observations to facilitate the prediction of future states, but end-to-end training of these models is nontrivial because representations may collapse if our only goal is to construct a latent state that is easy to predict. We introduce a sensorimotor world model (SMWM): a latent world model trained end-to-end with inverse dynamics regularization. This single regularizer addresses both issues: it prevents representation collapse and induces action-aligned representations. By forcing latent states to preserve information about the action underlying a transition, it biases the model toward the controllable degrees of freedom of the environment while discarding uncontrollable distractors. This yields stable latent world models trained from offline, reward-free trajectories, without frozen encoders, exponential moving averages, or complex latent regularizers. Empirically, SMWM learns compact, interpretable latent spaces and enables competitive planning performance across simple 2D and 3D control tasks.

### [72] [UltraQuant: 4-bit KV Caching for Context-Heavy Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20474v2)
*Inesh Chakrabarti,David Limpus,Aditi Ghai Rana,Bowen Bao,Spandan Tiwari,Thiago Crepaldi,Ashish Sirasao*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 4-bit KV缓存优化上下文重型agent，直接提升coding agent效率

TL;DR: 提出一种针对上下文密集型智能体的4位KV缓存压缩方法（UltraQuant），通过旋转、非对称处理、块尺度等设计，在AMD GPU上实现3.47倍首令牌延迟降低和1.63倍吞吐量提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 上下文密集型智能体导致KV缓存压力大，长前缀重复使用和高并发性使服务系统难保持GPU利用率，现有FP8缓存无法满足需求。

Method: 采用TurboQuant式旋转和码本量化，结合非对称K/V处理、Walsh-Hadamard旋转、移除QJL、块尺度变体，并在AMD GPU上使用FP4近似路径UltraQuant（FP8查询、FP4 KV、UE8M0组尺度、原生MFMA支持）及优化解码注意力核。

Result: 在长上下文多轮智能体工作负载中，P50首令牌延迟在后期轮次降低3.47倍（所有轮次平均2.3倍），输出吞吐量提升1.63倍（对比FP8 KV基线）。

Conclusion: 提出的4位KV缓存方法（UltraQuant）能有效缓解上下文密集型智能体的缓存压力，显著提升服务性能，且通过稳健设计选择实现高质量与吞吐量平衡。

中文摘要：上下文密集型智能体给键值（KV）缓存带来了异常压力：长前缀在许多短轮次中被重复使用，而并发性决定了服务系统能否保持GPU利用率。我们研究了在这种设置下的4位KV缓存压缩，使用TurboQuant风格的旋转和码本量化作为质量锚点，vLLM FP8 KV缓存作为部署锚点。我们报告了三个贡献。首先，我们将4位KV缓存框架化为多轮智能体工作负载，其中任务质量、缓存驻留和服务吞吐量必须联合测量。其次，我们描述了使4位路径稳健所需的实际设计选择，包括非对称K/V处理、Walsh-Hadamard旋转、QJL移除和块尺度变体。第三，我们介绍了在AMD GPU上的服务优化，包括优化的解码注意力核和UltraQuant，一种使用FP8查询、FP4 KV张量、UE8M0组尺度和CDNA4上原生缩放MFMA支持的FP4近似路径。在长上下文、多轮智能体工作负载中，UltraQuant在缓存压力大的后期轮次中将P50首令牌延迟降低了3.47倍（所有轮次平均降低2.3倍），并将输出吞吐量比FP8 KV基线提高了1.63倍。

Original abstract: Context-heavy agents place unusual pressure on the key-value (KV) cache: long prefixes are reused across many short turns, while concurrency determines whether the serving system can keep GPUs utilized. We study 4-bit KV-cache compression for this setting, using TurboQuant-style rotation and codebook quantization as a quality anchor and vLLM FP8 KV caching as the deployment anchor. We report three contributions. First, we frame 4-bit KV caching around multi-round agent workloads where task quality, cache residency, and serving throughput must be measured jointly. Second, we describe the practical design choices needed to make the 4-bit path robust, including asymmetric K/V treatment, Walsh-Hadamard rotation, QJL removal, and block-scale variants. Third, we present serving optimizations on AMD GPUs, including optimized decode-attention kernels and UltraQuant, an FP4 approximation path that uses FP8 queries, FP4 KV tensors, UE8M0 group scales, and native scaled-MFMA support on CDNA4. On a long-context, multi-turn agentic workload, UltraQuant cuts P50 time-to-first-token by 3.47x in the cache-pressured late rounds (2.3x across all rounds) and raises output throughput by 1.63x over the FP8 KV baseline.

### [73] [Contagion Networks: Evaluator Preference Propagation in Multi-Agent LLM Systems](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20493v2)
*Zewen Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 多agent系统中评估偏好传播，可迁移至coding agent协作评估

TL;DR: 提出Contagion Networks框架，发现LLM评估者偏好通过共享架构先验而非显式提示在智能体间传播，拓扑结构决定传播机制，增大评估委员会规模可有效缓解偏好传染。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多智能体系统中LLM评估者的偏好传播可能导致系统偏差放大，缺乏量化框架来理解和控制这一现象。

Method: 设计Contagion Networks框架，通过3智能体实验测量Cross-Agent Contagion Matrix，分析提示偏好与架构先验的贡献，研究不同拓扑（链式、全连接）和评估委员会规模的影响。

Result: 偏好持续传播（gamma 0.157-0.352）；架构先验主导传染（贡献63.5%）；链式拓扑抑制（beta=0.0126），全连接拓扑级联（Delta H=-0.020）；增加委员会规模k=1->3可降低68.9%传染。

Conclusion: LLM评估者偏好传播主要由共享架构先验驱动，拓扑是传播模式的关键决定因素，增大评估委员会规模是有效的缓解策略。

中文摘要：当大型语言模型在多智能体系统中担任评估者时，其策略偏好——无论是通过显式提示还是共享架构先验诱导的——会在智能体网络中传播。我们引入了传染网络（Contagion Networks），这是一个形式化框架，用于衡量评估者偏好如何在交互的LLM智能体之间传播。在使用DeepSeek-chat和三种不同的评估者偏好配置文件（结构化、平衡、基于证据）进行的受控3智能体实验中，我们测量了跨智能体传染矩阵Gamma_3，发现偏好始终在智能体之间传播（gamma在[0.157, 0.352]范围内）。一个中性提示对照实验揭示了一个反直觉的结果：共享架构先验作为传染的驱动因素主导了显式偏好提示（rho_neutral = 1.498 vs. rho_mixed = 1.299；提示贡献：-63.5%）。我们识别了由谱半径rho(Gamma_N)控制的三种传播机制，并证明相同的智能体在链式拓扑中抑制了偏好传染（beta_3 = 0.0126 +/- 0.0038，95% CI [0.0089, 0.0163]，n=4个种子），但在全连接拓扑中级联（Delta H_avg = -0.020）——这是一种依赖于拓扑的机制转换，在同类和跨模型智能体池（rho^cross = 1.296 +/- 0.016，n=4）中均得到验证。我们表明，将评估者委员会规模从k=1增加到k=3可将有效传染降低68.9% +/- 14.1%（n=4个种子），提供了一种可行的缓解策略。我们发布了开源的Contagion Network实验框架。

Original abstract: When large language models serve as evaluators in multi-agent systems, their strategy preferences -- whether induced by explicit prompts or by shared architectural priors -- propagate through the agent network. We introduce Contagion Networks, a formal framework for measuring how evaluator preferences spread across interacting LLM agents. In a controlled 3-agent experiment using DeepSeek-chat with three distinct evaluator preference profiles (structured, balanced, evidence-based), we measure the Cross-Agent Contagion Matrix Gamma_3 and find that preferences consistently propagate between agents (gamma in [0.157, 0.352]). A neutral-prompt control experiment reveals a counter-intuitive result: shared architectural priors dominate explicit preference prompts as the driver of contagion (rho_neutral = 1.498 vs. rho_mixed = 1.299; prompt contribution: -63.5%). We identify three propagation regimes governed by the spectral radius rho(Gamma_N) and demonstrate that the same agents suppress preference contagion in chain topology (beta_3 = 0.0126 +/- 0.0038, 95% CI [0.0089, 0.0163], n=4 seeds) but cascade in fully-connected topology (Delta H_avg = -0.020) -- a topology-dependent regime transition validated both for homogeneous and cross-model agent pools (rho^cross = 1.296 +/- 0.016, n=4). We show that increasing evaluator committee size from k=1 to k=3 reduces effective contagion by 68.9% +/- 14.1% (n=4 seeds), providing an actionable mitigation strategy. We release the open-source Contagion Network experimental framework.

</details>


### [74] [Is Our Benchmark Enough? An Analysis of Continual Learning for MLLMs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20961v1)
*Van-Tuan Tran,Shruthi Gowda,Merim Dzaferagic,Marco Ruffini*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 持续学习benchmark分析及路由方法，对agent持续适应有启发

TL;DR: 本文在MLLM持续学习领域，通过实验证明路由不需要MLLM、共享专家无效，并指出现有基准因任务高度可分离和固定任务顺序而存在结构缺陷，需重新设计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 重新审视MR-LoRA方法对MLLM路由器的依赖假设，并揭示MLLM-CL基准的结构性局限。

Method: 提出无需训练和重放的典型路由方法RePRo，并分析MLLM-CL基准的任务可分离性与固定任务顺序问题。

Result: RePRo以更低计算成本达到与MR-LoRA相当的路由性能；共享专家未带来性能提升；基准任务高可分离性和固定课程导致评估偏倚。

Conclusion: 现有基准侧重孤立学习，未来基准应引入重叠任务流形、多任务顺序、细粒度领域迁移及兼顾前后向迁移的评估指标。

中文摘要：持续适应对于部署在不断演化的领域中的多模态大语言模型（MLLMs）至关重要，但最先进的MR-LoRA方法高度依赖于一个假设，即基于MLLM的路由器对于处理复杂的多模态输入是必要的。本文在MLLM-CL基准上重新审视了这一论断，并提出了两个主张。第一，路由不需要MLLM：一种简单的无需训练、无需重放的典型路由方法（RePRo），使用冻结的预训练特征和任务原型，以更低的计算成本匹配MR-LoRA的基于MLLM的路由器。第二，共享专家并不能改善MLLMs的持续学习，尽管它们在理论上具有吸引力。我们表明，这些发现源于MLLM-CL的两个结构限制：（1）其任务在表示空间中高度可分离，（2）其固定的任务顺序使得结论对单一课程敏感，而不是在各种持续学习轨迹上保持稳健。因此，该基准主要奖励孤立学习，而非真正的持续迁移。这激励了未来持续MLLM学习基准的新设计，包括重叠的任务流形、多个任务顺序、细粒度的领域转移，以及奖励前向迁移和保留的评估协议。

Original abstract: Continual adaptation is essential for multimodal large language models (MLLMs) deployed across evolving domains, but the state-of-the-art MR-LoRA method highly relies on the assumption that a MLLM-based router is necessary to process complex multimodal inputs. This paper revisits this claim on the MLLM-CL benchmark and argues for two claims. \textbf{First}, routing does not require an MLLM: a simple training-free, replay-free ptotypical routing method (\textsc{RePRo}), uses frozen pretrained features and task prototypes to match the MLLM-based router of MR-LoRA at far lower computational cost. \textbf{Second}, shared experts do not improve continual learning for MLLMs, despite their theoretical appeal. We show that these findings arise from two structural limitations of MLLM-CL: (1) its tasks are \textbf{highly separable} in representation space, and (2) its fixed task order makes conclusions \textbf{sensitive to a single curriculum} rather than robust across diverse continual-learning trajectories. As a result, the benchmark primarily rewards learning in isolation rather than genuine continual transfer. This motivates a new design for future benchmarks of continual MLLM learning, with overlapping task manifolds, multiple task orders, fine-grained domain shifts, and evaluation protocols that reward forward transfer as well as retention.

</details>

# cs.CV [[Back]](#toc)

### [75] [See-and-Reach: Precise Vision-Language Navigation for UAVs within the Field of View](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20045v1)
*Fanfu Xue,En Yu,Yantian Shen,Zhikun Hu,Hongjun Wang,Yang Yang,Xindi Wang,Jiande Sun*

Main category: cs.CV

Selection reason: UAV视觉语言导航agent，具体领域但可视为embodied agent。

TL;DR: 针对无人机视觉语言导航中难以评估目标可见时的精确到达能力的问题，提出UAV-VLN-FOV任务和3DG-VLN框架，通过动态3D方向引导的航点预测，在仿真和真实环境中取得显著性能提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有UAV-VLN将远程搜索和最终到达联合优化，难以单独评估无人机在目标可见时的视觉定位和精确运动能力，需要专门的任务和框架来诊断终端到达能力。

Method: 提出3DG-VLN框架，利用动态3D方向线索引导航点预测；自适应处理高分辨率前视和下视图像，保留细粒度视觉和几何信息；在线更新目标相对方向，减少漂移；并构建包含2717条轨迹的高分辨率基准。

Result: 在基准测试中，3DG-VLN相比基线方法成功率达到13.82%的提升，真实世界试验验证了其实用性。

Conclusion: 3DG-VLN通过针对性的任务设计和动态方向引导，有效提升了无人机在目标可见情况下的精确导航能力，为实际应用提供了潜力。

中文摘要：无人机视觉语言导航（UAV-VLN）通常被建模为一个整体的搜索与到达问题，其中远程目标发现和最终目标接近被联合优化和评估。这种表述使得评估空中具身智能体的一项关键能力变得困难，即一旦目标进入其视野，无人机能否准确地将可见目标进行视觉定位并将视觉语言证据转化为精确的三维运动。为了解决这一局限性，我们引入了UAV-VLN-FOV，一个目标可见导航任务，该任务孤立了“看见并到达”阶段，并能够对终端到达能力进行更具诊断性的评估。我们进一步提出了3DG-VLN，一种由动态3D方向线索引导的视觉语言航点预测框架，以增强细粒度视觉定位和空间方向对齐，从而实现精确的目标到达。具体来说，3DG-VLN自适应地处理高分辨率前视和下视观测，以保留用于目标定位的细粒度视觉和几何细节。它还在闭环导航过程中在线更新目标相对方向，使智能体能够保持与目标的空间对齐，并减少累积的方向漂移。为了支持该任务，我们构建了一个专用的高分辨率基准，包含2,717条轨迹，每条轨迹包含面向目标的高级指令、高分辨率前视和下视自我中心观测以及连续的三维航点标注。实验表明，3DG-VLN优于具有竞争力的UAV-VLN基线，成功率达到13.82%的提升。真实世界试验进一步展示了3DG-VLN在实际“看见并到达”导航中的潜力。源代码和基准可在https://github.com/xuefanfu/3DG-VLN获取。

Original abstract: UAV Vision-Language Navigation (UAV-VLN) is typically formulated as a holistic search-and-reach problem, where long-range target discovery and final target approach are optimized and evaluated jointly. This formulation makes it difficult to assess a critical capability of aerial embodied agents, namely whether a UAV can accurately ground a visible target and translate vision-language evidence into precise 3D motion once the target enters its field of view. To address this limitation, we introduce UAV-VLN-FOV, a target-visible navigation task that isolates the see-and-reach stage and enables a more diagnostic evaluation of terminal reaching ability. We further propose 3DG-VLN, a vision-language waypoint prediction framework guided by dynamic 3D direction cues to enhance fine-grained visual grounding and spatial direction alignment for precise target reaching. Specifically, 3DG-VLN adaptively processes high-resolution front-view and downward-view observations to preserve fine-grained visual and geometric details for target grounding. It also updates the target-relative direction online during closed-loop navigation, allowing the agent to maintain spatial alignment with the target and reduce accumulated direction drift. To support this task, we construct a dedicated high-resolution benchmark which contains 2,717 trajectories with target-oriented high-level instructions, high-resolution front-view and downward-view egocentric observations, and continuous 3D waypoint annotations. Experiments show that 3DG-VLN outperforms competitive UAV-VLN baselines, achieving a 13.82\% improvement in success rate. Real-world trials further demonstrate the potential of 3DG-VLN for practical see-and-reach navigation. The source code and benchmark are available at https://github.com/xuefanfu/3DG-VLN.

</details>


### [76] [GroundShot: Visually Consistent Multi-Shot Long Video Generation via Entity-Grounded Shot Scheduling](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20799v2)
*Yixuan Lai,Tianjia Shao,Kun Zhou,Weijia Dou,Siyu Zhu,Jingdong Wang*

Main category: cs.CV

Selection reason: 提出基于实体记忆和调度的agentic框架，可启发agent的长期记忆和引用机制。

TL;DR: 提出GroundShot框架，通过在线构建实体级视觉记忆，无需训练即可提升多镜头视频生成的实体一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多镜头视频中实体一致性随镜头增加而累积漂移，而观众以实体的首次清晰出现为判断基准，因此需要以实体为中心的方法来维持一致性。

Method: GroundShot在线从已接受生成镜头中建立实体记忆，动态安排生成顺序，提取并验证实体可靠性，在生成前检索合适参考。

Result: 在GroundBench基准上，GroundShot显著提升多镜头一致性，且无需额外训练或模型修改。

Conclusion: GroundShot有效解决了多镜头视频中的实体一致性问题，是一种灵活且高效的框架。

中文摘要：生成视觉一致的多镜头视频仍然是一个开放挑战。随着视频包含更多镜头，镜头间的不一致性会累积，导致在多个镜头中重复出现的实体（角色、物体和地点）偏离其首次出现的样子。我们观察到，观众通过将实体的每次后续出现与其首次清晰出现进行比较来判断一致性；初次出现的视觉质量设定了后续所有出现的一致性上限。受此启发，我们提出了GroundShot，一个无需训练、模型无关的智能体框架，用于基于实体的多镜头生成。GroundShot从已接受的生成镜头中在线构建实体级视觉记忆：它根据镜头作为实体参考的预期有用性来安排其生成顺序，从生成的视频中提取实体，在添加到记忆前验证其可靠性，并在每个镜头生成前从记忆中检索合适的实体参考。为了评估这种以实体为中心的一致性观点，我们进一步引入了GroundBench，一个诊断基准，用于在实体层面测量一致性，同时隔离受控的挑战维度。实验表明，GroundShot在不需额外训练或模型修改的情况下，提高了多镜头一致性。

Original abstract: Generating visually consistent multi-shot videos remains an open challenge. As videos span more shots, inconsistencies can accumulate across shots, causing entities that reappear across shots -- characters, objects, and locations -- to drift away from how they first appear. We observe that viewers judge consistency by comparing each later appearance of an entity with its first clear appearance; the visual quality of this initial appearance sets the consistency ceiling for all that follows. Motivated by this, we present \textbf{GroundShot}, a training-free, model-agnostic agentic framework for entity-grounded multi-shot generation. GroundShot builds an entity-level visual memory online from accepted generated shots: it schedules shots' generation order by their expected usefulness as entity references, grounds entities from generated videos, verifies their reliability before adding them to memory, and retrieves suitable entity references from memory before each shot is generated. To evaluate this entity-centered view of consistency, we further introduce \textbf{GroundBench}, a diagnostic benchmark that measures consistency at the entity level while isolating controlled challenge dimensions. Experiments show that GroundShot improves multi-shot consistency over existing methods while requiring no additional training or model modification.

</details>

### [77] [DataMagic: Transforming Tabular Data into Data Insight Video](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20388v1)
*Yupeng Xie,Chen Ma,Zhenyang Wang,Liangwei Wang,Jiayi Zhu,Chuxuan Zeng,Zhouan Shen,Boyan Li,Yuyu Luo*

Main category: cs.HC

Selection reason: 多agent架构生成数据视频，agent协作通用方法可跟踪

TL;DR: DataMagic是一个端到端交互系统，能将原始表格数据和自然语言查询转化为数据叙事视频，通过声明式规范DVSpec确保数据保真度，并采用多智能体架构解决设计空间组合爆炸问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有数据视频制作工具或缺乏叙事逻辑和动画（如BI仪表板），或需要预准备可视化而非从原始数据出发，或无法保证数据保真度和来源可追溯性（如像素级视频生成模型）。

Method: 提出DataMagic系统，包含声明式规范DVSpec（绑定视觉/动画元素到数据字段）和Generate-then-Orchestrate多智能体架构（并行生成场景再全局编排），并支持三种交互模式和来源可溯数据问答。

Result: 在109个真实样本上验证了DataMagic的有效性。

Conclusion: DataMagic通过端到端方式将原始表格数据转化为交互式数据叙事视频，保证了数据保真度和叙事连贯性，为数据视频制作提供了有效解决方案。

中文摘要：数据视频将动态图表、语音叙述和同步动画整合为时间性叙事来传达数据洞察，使其成为提高数据管理生命周期中数据消费效率的有效媒介。然而，制作高质量的数据视频需要涵盖数据分析、叙事设计和视频制作的专业知识。现有方法存在不足：静态可视化工具（如BI仪表板）缺乏叙事逻辑和动画；创作工具需要用户预先准备可视化，而非从原始数据出发；像素级视频生成模型无法保证数据保真度和来源可追溯性。我们展示了DataMagic，一个端到端的交互系统，能够将原始表格数据和自然语言查询转化为叙事性数据洞察视频。为确保数据保真度，DataMagic引入了声明式规范DVSpec，通过数据驱动的语义引用将视觉和动画元素与底层数据字段绑定。为了解决设计空间的组合爆炸问题，DataMagic采用了一种“先生成后编排”的多智能体架构，并行生成候选场景，然后通过全局编排优化叙事连贯性。利用DVSpec的逻辑与渲染解耦特性，该系统进一步支持三种交互模式和基于结构化来源的数据问答，将单向视频转变为可探索的交互式数据界面。在109个真实样本上的评估验证了DataMagic的有效性。主页：https://datamagic-home.github.io/

Original abstract: Data videos integrate dynamic charts, voice narration, and synchronized animations to communicate data insights as temporal narratives, making them an effective medium for improving data consumption efficiency in the data management lifecycle. However, producing high-quality data videos requires expertise spanning data analysis, narrative design, and video production. Existing approaches fall short: static visualization tools (e.g., BI dashboards) lack narrative logic and animation; authoring tools require users to pre-prepare visualizations rather than working from raw data; pixel-level video generation models cannot guarantee data fidelity or provenance. We demonstrate DataMagic, an end-to-end interactive system that transforms raw tabular data and natural language queries into narrative data-insight videos. To ensure data fidelity, DataMagic introduces the declarative specification DVSpec, which binds visual and animation elements to underlying data fields through data-driven semantic references. To address the combinatorial explosion of the design space, DataMagic adopts a Generate-then-Orchestrate multi-agent architecture that generates candidate scenes in parallel and then optimizes narrative coherence through global orchestration. Leveraging DVSpec's decoupling of logic and rendering, the system further supports three interaction modes and structured provenance-based data Q&A, transforming one-way videos into explorable interactive data interfaces. Evaluation on 109 real-world samples validates the effectiveness of the DataMagic. Homepage: https://datamagic-home.github.io/

### [78] [Artificial collectives of specialists and generalists excel at different tasks](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20877v1)
*John Meluso,Laurent Hébert-Dufresne,Christoph Riedl,H. Oliver Gao*

Main category: cs.MA

Selection reason: 研究多agent系统中专才与通才的性能权衡，对agent团队设计有指导意义。

TL;DR: 通过系统实验揭示了智能体的解释能力、理性边界和任务质量如何相互作用影响集体性能，并提出了解释网络与任务需求和计算限制相匹配的设计原则。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管多智能体系统有大量工程解决方案，但缺乏描述性科学理解，导致难以设计资源高效的集体。

Method: 采用优化智能体进行系统实验，改变智能体的解释能力（从专家到通才）、理性边界（宽松到严格）和任务质量，观察集体性能的变化。

Result: 解释网络属性平均影响小（0.07 sd），但对特定任务影响大（可达1.84 sd）；通才集体在生成、选择和协调任务上更优，专家集体（加通才调解者）在谈判任务上更优；理性边界调节关系：宽松边界下专家更优，严格边界下通才更优，中等边界下存在权衡。

Conclusion: 多智能体设计应匹配解释网络与任务需求和计算限制，以提高效率和降低能源成本。

中文摘要：集体人工智能，其中多个智能体在共享任务上工作，具有解决从医学到集体治理等领域中广泛问题的潜力。但是，虽然规范性工程解决方案比比皆是，我们缺乏对人工集体的描述性科学理解，因此也缺乏如何设计资源高效的多智能体系统的原则。通过使用优化智能体的系统实验，我们表征了智能体的解释能力、理性边界和任务质量如何相互作用以塑造集体性能。智能体从具有狭窄解释能力的专家到具有广泛解释能力的通才不等。专家集体对应于稀疏的、中心化的网络，而通才集体对应于密集的、去中心化的网络。我们表明，解释网络属性平均对性能的影响很小（性能的0.07个标准差）。然而，对于特定的任务质量，这些影响要大4.5倍（0.33个标准差），并且对于某些任务质量可以达到更高（1.84个标准差）。这导致通才集体在涉及生成、选择和协调的任务上表现更好，而带有少数通才调解者的专家集体在涉及谈判的任务上表现更好。理性边界则调节这些关系。在宽松边界下，专家通过更高效地采样高维决策空间而优于通才。在严格边界下，通才通过更好的梯度估计而优于专家。在中等边界下，性能与收敛速度之间出现了基本的权衡。这些发现表明，多智能体设计可能受益于将解释网络与任务需求和智能体的计算限制相匹配，这对多智能体系统的效率和能源成本具有影响。

Original abstract: Collective artificial intelligence, where multiple agents work on shared tasks, holds potential to solve expansive problems in fields from medicine to collective governance. But while prescriptive engineering solutions abound, we lack descriptive scientific understanding of artificial collectives, and therefore principles for how to design resource efficient multi-agent systems. Through systematic experiments with optimizing agents, we characterize how agent interpretive abilities, rationality bounds, and task qualities interact to shape collective performance. Agents range from specialists, with narrow interpretive abilities, to generalists, with broad ones. Collectives of specialists correspond to sparse, centralized networks, while collectives of generalists correspond to dense, decentralized ones. We show that interpretive network properties have small performance effects on average (0.07 standard deviations of performance). However, for specific task qualities, these effects are 4.5 times larger (0.33 sd) and can reach much higher for certain task qualities (1.84 sd). This leads collectives of generalists to perform better on tasks that involve generating, choosing, and coordinating, while collectives of specialists with a few generalist mediators perform better on tasks that involve negotiating. Rationality bounds then moderate these relationships. At loose bounds, specialists outperform generalists through more effective sampling of high-dimensional decision spaces. At tight bounds, generalists outperform specialists through better gradient estimation. A fundamental trade-off between performance and convergence speed emerges at moderate bounds. These findings suggest that multi-agent design could benefit from matching interpretive networks to both task demands and agents' computational limits, with implications for the efficiency and energy costs of multi-agent systems.

</details>

### [79] [Optimal Order of Multi-Agent and General Many-Body Systems](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20485v1)
*Jake J. Xia*

Main category: q-fin.RM

Selection reason: 多agent系统理论框架，可迁移至协作agent设计

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个基于权力和响应函数的通用框架，用于分析多智能体系统中的反馈循环，推导出宏观属性，并研究了增长与韧性之间的权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究缺乏一个统一的框架来解释多智能体系统中微观变量与宏观涌现属性之间的关系，特别是如何平衡集体增长与系统韧性。

Method: 构建基于权力和响应函数的通用框架，利用数学推导建立宏观属性与微观变量的关系，并引入风险偏好参数化的效用函数分析最优秩序。

Result: 推导出总权力、有用权力、熵、秩序、脆弱性和流动性等宏观属性的表达式；发现更强的同步性提高产出但增加脆弱性；秩序和熵等概念是任务相关的。

Conclusion: 通过测量和设计权力分布与响应函数，可以优化集体行为，实现集体智能和最优秩序，为理解和预测多智能体系统提供新途径。

中文摘要：本文开发了一个通用框架，用于分析具有代理行为与集体观测之间反馈循环的多智能体系统。该框架建立在两个基本的智能体级变量上：权力，衡量智能体对集体结果的影响；以及响应函数，决定智能体如何对观测做出反应。我们推导了宏观属性，包括总权力、有用权力、熵、秩序、脆弱性和流动性，如何从异质智能体的这两个变量中涌现出来。为了研究增长与韧性之间的权衡，我们引入了一个由风险偏好系数参数化的系统级效用函数，并推导出平衡生产力、稳定性和适应性的最优秩序程度。分析表明，更强的同步性可以提高集体产出，但也可能增加系统脆弱性并降低流动性。我们进一步论证，秩序、熵、信息和有用能量是任务依赖和系统相对的概念，其含义取决于系统的目标。通过测量和设计智能体的权力分布和响应函数，可能更好地理解、预测和优化集体行为，并识别集体智能和最优秩序出现的条件。

Original abstract: This paper develops a general framework for analyzing multi-agent systems with feedback loops between agents actions and collective observations. The framework is built on two fundamental agent-level variables: power, which measures agent influence on collective outcomes, and response functions, which determine how agents react to observations. We derive how macroscopic properties, including total power, useful power, entropy, order, fragility, and mobility, emerge from these two variables of heterogeneous agents. To study the trade off between growth and resilience, we introduce a system-level utility function parameterized by a risk-appetite coefficient and derive an optimal degree of order that balances productivity, stability, and adaptability. The analysis suggests that stronger synchronization can increase collective output but may also increase systemic fragility and reduce mobility. We further argue that order, entropy, information, and useful energy are task-dependent and system-relative concepts whose meanings depend on the objectives of the system. By measuring and designing agent power distributions and response functions, it may be possible to better understand, predict, and optimize collective behavior and identify the conditions under which collective intelligence and optimal order emerge.

</details>

### [80] [SafeSpec: Fast and Safe LLM via Dynamic Reflective Sampling](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19755v1)
*Haotian Xu,Zeyang Zhang,Linbao Li,Huadi Zheng,Yu Li,Cheng Zhuo*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: 安全推测解码框架，涉及agent安全与效率。

TL;DR: SafeSpec通过在推测性解码中集成风险估计，实现了安全与效率的联合优化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有安全方法与推测性解码不兼容，要么增加计算开销，要么破坏加速机制，亟需一种能同时保证安全和解码加速的方法。

Method: 在目标模型上附加轻量级潜在安全头，单次前向传递中联合评估语义有效性和安全性；检测到不安全时，采用回滚和安全引导的反射多重采样恢复安全延续。

Result: 在多个模型和基准上，攻击成功率降低15%，同时保持2.06倍推理加速。

Conclusion: 推测性加速和推理时安全性可以共同优化，SafeSpec实现了更好的安全-效率权衡。

中文摘要：推测性推理加速了大语言模型（LLM）的解码速度，但本身不提供安全保障。现有的安全防御措施与推测性推理大多不兼容：它们要么引入额外的计算，要么破坏草稿-验证机制，从而抵消加速优势。这揭示了当前安全方法与推测性解码之间的根本性不兼容。我们提出了SafeSpec，一个安全感知的推测性推理框架，将风险估计直接集成到验证过程中。SafeSpec在目标模型上附加一个轻量级的潜在安全头，以在单次前向传递中联合评估语义有效性和安全性。当检测到不安全生成时，SafeSpec应用回滚和安全引导的反射多重采样来恢复安全的延续，而不是终止生成。我们将越狱攻击建模为生成轨迹上的分布偏移，其中对抗性提示增加了有害延续的概率，但并未消除安全延续。在该模型下，SafeSpec在推测性解码过程中执行风险感知的轨迹恢复。在多个模型和对抗性基准测试中，SafeSpec实现了显著改进的安全-效率权衡。在Qwen3-32B上，SafeSpec将攻击成功率降低了15%，同时在良性工作负载上保持了2.06倍的推理加速，表明推测性加速和推理时安全性可以共同优化。

Original abstract: Speculative inference accelerates large language model (LLM) decoding but provides no inherent safety guarantees. Existing safety defenses are largely incompatible with speculative inference: they either introduce additional computation or disrupt the draft-verify mechanism, negating acceleration benefits. This reveals a fundamental incompatibility between current safety methods and speculative decoding. We propose SafeSpec, a safety-aware speculative inference framework that integrates risk estimation directly into the verification process. SafeSpec attaches a lightweight latent safety head to the target model to jointly evaluate semantic validity and safety in a single forward pass. When unsafe generations are detected, SafeSpec applies rollback and safety-guided reflective multi-sampling to recover safe continuations rather than terminating generation. We model jailbreak attacks as distributional shifts over generative trajectories, where adversarial prompts increase the probability of harmful continuations without eliminating safe ones. Under this model, SafeSpec performs risk-aware trajectory recovery within the speculative decoding process. Across multiple models and adversarial benchmarks, SafeSpec achieves a substantially improved safety-efficiency trade-off. On Qwen3-32B, SafeSpec reduces attack success rates by 15% while preserving a 2.06x inference speedup on benign workloads, demonstrating that speculative acceleration and inference-time safety can be jointly optimized.

</details>


### [81] [NRT-Bench: Benchmarking Multi-Turn Red-Teaming of LLM Operator Agents in Safety-Critical Control Rooms](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20408v3)
*Hanwool Lee,Dasol Choi,Bokyeong Kim,Haon Park,Seung Geun Kim*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: 多轮红队攻击LLM agent安全基准，可迁移至coding agent安全评估

TL;DR: 提出NRT-Bench基准，评估LLM智能体作为核电站操作员在自适应多轮攻击下的鲁棒性，发现攻击可靠导致安全功能失效，模型间漏洞几乎不重叠，且防御效果高度模型依赖。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM智能体被用于安全关键系统监督，但其在持续自适应对抗下的鲁棒性尚未得到充分研究。

Method: 构建模拟核电站控制室环境，采用五角色操作员团队（每个由LLM驱动）、六项CSF、四个攻击通道，通过固定攻击对等重放协议评估四个前沿LLM模型。

Result: 自适应多轮攻击成功率8.7%-12.1%；模型间失败几乎不重叠（149个攻击会话中无同时击败全部模型的情况）；添加防御效果因模型而异，同一防御可提高或降低攻击成功率。

Conclusion: LLM智能体在安全关键任务中存在显著且模型特定的脆弱性，防御需针对性设计；发布仿真与数据工具促进可重复研究。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）智能体越来越多地被提议作为安全关键系统的监督组件，但它们在持续、自适应对抗压力下的鲁棒性仍然缺乏充分表征。我们提出了NRT-Bench，这是一个针对LLM智能体作为安全关键系统操作员的多轮红队基准测试，实例化在模拟核电站控制室中。一个由五个角色组成的操作员团队，每个角色由一个可配置的LLM支持，运行一个受六项关键安全功能（CSF）管理的核电站，同时对抗者通过四个通道在有界多轮会话中注入消息，每轮都有反馈。伤害是一个客观信号而非LLM判断的文本：一旦任何CSF丢失，运行立即终止，并归因于导致该结果的消息。在固定攻击对等重放协议下评估四个前沿操作员模型，我们发现自适应多轮攻击可靠地将操作员团队推过安全极限：在四个模型中，8.7%到12.1%的攻击会话以核电站失去一项关键安全功能结束。尽管按此总比率看四个模型几乎同样鲁棒，但它们的失败几乎没有重叠：在149个会话中，没有一个会话同时击败所有四个模型，而三分之一击败了至少一个，因此漏洞在不同模型之间几乎是分离的，而非嵌套的。添加防御的效果强烈依赖于模型：同一个护栏堆栈或安全顾问智能体可以降低一个模型的攻击成功率，却提高另一个模型的成功率。我们发布了仿真环境、攻击数据集和重放工具，以实现LLM智能体可重复的安全性评估。

Original abstract: Large language model (LLM) agents are increasingly proposed as supervisory components for safety-critical systems, yet their robustness under sustained, adaptive adversarial pressure remains poorly characterized. We present NRT-Bench, a benchmark for multi-turn red-teaming of LLM agents acting as operators of a safety-critical system, instantiated in a simulated nuclear power plant control room. A five-role operator team, each backed by a configurable LLM, runs a plant governed by six critical safety functions (CSFs), while adversaries inject messages over four channels in bounded multi-turn sessions with per-turn feedback. Harm is an objective signal rather than LLM-judged text: a run terminates the moment any CSF is lost, attributed to the causing message. Evaluating four frontier operator models under a fixed-attack paired-replay protocol, we find that adaptive multi-turn attacks reliably push the operator team past a safety limit: across the four models, between 8.7% and 12.1% of attack sessions end with the plant losing a critical safety function. Although the four models look almost equally robust by this aggregate rate, their failures barely overlap: of $149$ sessions, none defeat all four models while a third defeat at least one, so vulnerabilities are nearly disjoint across models rather than nested. The effect of added defences is strongly model-dependent: the same guardrail stack or safety-advisor agent that lowers attack success for one model can raise it for another. We release the simulation venue, attack dataset, and replay tooling for reproducible safety evaluation of LLM agents.

</details>


### [82] [Image Encryption Algorithm Based on Convolutional Neural Networks and Dynamic S-Box Generation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20444v1)
*Ans Ibrahim Mahameed,Fadhil Abbas Fadhil,Maryam Mahdi Alhusseini,Mohammad-Reza Feizi-Derakhshi,Nikolai Safiullin*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 提出一种动态图像加密方法，利用CNN生成自适应S-box，提高非线性、唯一性和抗攻击能力，安全性优于传统方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统固定S-box易受线性攻击和差分攻击，需要更安全、灵活的图像加密方法。

Method: 结合CNN和经典密码学，通过CNN学习图像特征生成自适应S-box，用于像素替换。

Result: 基于CNN的S-box具有更高的非线性、唯一性和输入依赖性，安全性评估指标（熵、相关性、NPCR、UACI）显示方案更鲁棒和灵活。

Conclusion: 所提动态图像加密方案比传统方法更安全、更具弹性，能有效抵抗统计和结构攻击。

中文摘要：本文提出了一种动态图像加密方法，结合卷积神经网络（CNN）和经典密码学，以提高图像加密的安全性和灵活性。主要概念是基于训练好的CNN学习到的特征创建自适应替换盒（S-box）。与传统的固定S-box相比，基于CNN的S-box具有更高的非线性、唯一性和输入图像依赖性，因为它们易受线性攻击和差分攻击。这种动态行为增强了混淆特性，使其更能抵抗统计攻击和结构攻击。加密算法包括基于CNN的特征提取和创建个性化S-box来替换像素。通过熵、直方图分析、相关性、NPCR和UACI等指标对生成的基于CNN的S-box进行安全评估，表明该方案比传统方案更具弹性和灵活性。

Original abstract: The paper proposes a dynamic approach to image encryption, combining the use of Convolutional Neural Networks (CNNs) and classical cryptography to improve the security and flexibility of image encryption. The main concept is to create adaptive Substitution boxes (S-boxes) based on characteristics that are learned by a trained CNN. The CNN-based S-boxes can be relied on for more non-linearity, uniqueness, and input image dependence than the conventional fixed S-boxes because they are susceptible to the linear and differential attacks. This dynamic behaviour enhances the confusion property and makes it more resistant to statistical and structural attacks. The encryption algorithm consists of CNN-based feature extraction and the creation of a personalised S-box to replace the pixels. Entropy, histogram analysis, correlation, NPCR, and UACI enable security assessment of generated S-boxes based on the CNN, indicating that the scheme is more resilient and flexible than traditional ones.

### [83] [Analyzing Defensive Misdirection Against Model-Guided Automated Attacks on Agentic AI Systems](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20470v2)
*Reza Soosahabi,Vivek Namsani*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: 防御性误导策略对抗自动攻击，可迁移至coding agent安全防御

TL;DR: 本文通过概率模型分析智能体AI系统的攻击-防御场景，提出检测-误导策略并使用CMPE方法，将越狱攻击成功率上限降低两个数量级，几乎消除攻击成功。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统检测-阻断防御因提供可预测拒绝而辅助自动化搜索，导致攻击成功率随查询预算增加而接近1，亟需更有效的防御策略。

Method: 建立目标系统、防御机制和攻击者评估器的概率模型，分析检测-阻断的局限，提出检测-误导策略；实现CMPE方法，用安全但误导性的响应替换拒绝文本，诱导攻击者评估器产生假阳性错误。

Result: 在越狱基准测试中，CMPE将估计的ASR上限降低两个数量级，并在PAIR和GPTFuzz攻击中几乎消除成功攻击。

Conclusion: 检测-误导策略能有效限制攻击成功率的渐近上界，CMPE作为轻量级实现，在自动化越狱场景中显著提升防御效果。

中文摘要：智能体AI系统越来越依赖语言模型组件来解读指令、处理外部数据、调用工具以及与其他智能体协调。这些能力使得提示注入和越狱攻击更具影响力，尤其是当攻击者采用模型引导的自动化来扩展探测、优化提示和评估响应时。本文通过一个目标系统、其防御机制以及攻击者的自动评估器的概率模型来分析由此产生的攻击-防御场景。我们的分析表明，传统的检测-阻断防御可能使攻击成功率（ASR）随着查询预算的增加而接近1，因为可预测的拒绝为自动化搜索提供了有用的反馈。然后我们研究了检测-误导策略，其中被检测到的恶意交互会收到受控的、非操作的响应，旨在诱导攻击者的评估器产生假阳性错误。该策略降低了攻击者选择候选的正预测值，并产生一个有界的渐近ASR。我们通过渐进式参与的情境误导（CMPE）评估了该策略的概念验证实现，这是一种轻量级的对话误导方法，旨在在自动化越狱环境中用安全但战略上具有误导性的响应替换可预测的拒绝文本。在越狱基准测试中，CMPE将估计的ASR上限降低了多达两个数量级，并且在端到端的PAIR和GPTFuzz攻击运行中几乎消除了已验证的攻击成功。

Original abstract: Agentic AI systems increasingly rely on language-model components to interpret instructions, process external data, invoke tools, and coordinate with other agents. These capabilities make prompt-injection and jailbreak attacks more consequential, especially as attackers adopt model-guided automation to scale probing, prompt refinement, and response evaluation. This work analyzes the resulting attack-defense setting through a probabilistic model of a target system, its defense mechanism, and the attacker's automated judge. Our analysis shows that conventional detect-and-block defenses can allow attacker success rate (ASR) to approach one as the query budget grows, since predictable refusals provide useful feedback to automated search. We then examine detect-and-misdirect, where detected malicious interactions receive controlled, non-operational responses designed to induce false-positive errors in the attacker's judge. This strategy reduces the positive predictive value of attacker-selected candidates and yields a bounded asymptotic ASR. We evaluate a proof-of-concept realization of this strategy through Contextual Misdirection via Progressive Engagement (CMPE), a lightweight conversational misdirection method designed to replace predictable refusal text with safe but strategically misleading responses in automated jailbreak settings. On jailbreak benchmarks, CMPE reduces estimated ASR upper bounds by up to two orders of magnitude and nearly eliminates verified attack success in end-to-end PAIR and GPTFuzz attack runs.

### [84] [Calibration Without Comprehension: Diagnosing the Limits of Fine-Tuning LLMs for Vulnerability Detection in Systems Software](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20502v1)
*Arastoo Zibaeirad,Marco Vieira*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 研究发现，当前LLMs在系统软件漏洞检测中缺乏真正的安全推理能力，数据污染无显著帮助，微调仅调整输出阈值而未改变决策策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决LLMs在漏洞基准测试中的高分是源于真实安全推理还是对污染数据的模式匹配这一未解决问题。

Method: 构建CWE-Trace框架，包含834个手动整理的Linux内核样本（74个CWE），采用严格时间分割（历史集/截止后无泄漏集），保留上下文感知的漏洞-补丁对，引入DFI和HDD两个诊断指标，评估8个原始LLM和15个LoRA微调变体在非目标检测、目标检测和CWE分类上的表现。

Result: 两个关键结果：1）数据污染无优势，84%的被污染样本无可用的记忆信号，31%存在CWE误分类；2）骨干方向性先验主导微调，模型失败模式稳定（DFI范围-85.5至+94.8pp），微调仅改变输出阈值，未改变决策策略。最佳检测分数仅52.1%（比随机高2.1pp），精确CWE Top-1准确率低于1.3%。

Conclusion: 当前LLMs缺乏对系统软件的可靠安全推理能力，检测与理解是解耦的，无论微调策略如何，均无法实现真正的安全推理。

中文摘要：LLMs在漏洞基准测试上得分高是否真正推理了安全性，还是仅仅对污染数据进行模式匹配，这一问题仍未解决。我们提出了CWE-Trace，一个用于LLM漏洞检测的框架，由834个手动整理的Linux内核样本构建，涵盖74个CWE。该框架强制进行严格的时间分割（2025年前历史集/截止后无泄漏集），保留上下文感知的漏洞-补丁对，并引入了两个诊断指标：方向性失败指数（DFI）和层次距离与方向（HDD）。我们评估了八个原始LLM和15个LoRA微调变体，涉及非目标检测、目标检测和CWE分类。我们的分析得出两个关键结果。首先，数据污染没有带来可测量的优势。函数级分析显示，84%的名义上被污染的样本不带有任何可用的记忆信号：漏洞函数缺失或在数据集间交叉映射，约31%的被污染样本存在CWE误分类。其次，骨干方向性先验主导了微调。模型表现出稳定、系统性的失败模式（DFI范围从-85.5到+94.8个百分点），这些模式从历史数据延续到截止后数据，且难以纠正。微调改变了输出阈值，但没有改变决策策略。这是无理解的校准：输出分布适应训练数据，而底层安全推理仍然缺失。在二分类检测中最弱的骨干（DeepSeek-R1）在粗粒度CWE分类中获益最多，揭示了检测和理解是解耦的能力。最佳检测分数仅达到52.1%（比随机高2.1个百分点）；精确CWE排序的Top-1准确率低于1.3%，确认了当前LLMs缺乏对系统软件的可靠安全推理，无论采用何种微调策略。

Original abstract: Whether LLMs scoring well on vulnerability benchmarks genuinely reason about security or merely pattern-match on contaminated data remains unresolved. We present CWE-Trace, a framework for LLM vulnerability detection built from 834 manually curated Linux kernel samples spanning 74 CWEs. The framework enforces a strict temporal split (pre-2025 historical set / post-cutoff leakage-free set), preserves context-aware vulnerable--patched pairs, and introduces two diagnostic metrics: the Directional Failure Index (DFI) and Hierarchical Distance and Direction (HDD). We evaluate eight vanilla LLMs and 15 LoRA fine-tuned variants across non-targeted detection, targeted detection, and CWE classification. Our analysis yields two key results. First, data contamination provides no measurable advantage. Function-level analysis shows that 84% of nominally contaminated samples carry no usable memorization signal: vulnerable functions are absent or cross-mapped across datasets, and ~31% of contaminated samples carry CWE misclassification. Second, backbone directional priors dominate fine-tuning. Models exhibit stable, systematic failure modes (DFI ranging from -85.5 to +94.8 pp) that persist from historical to post-cutoff data and resist correction. Fine-tuning shifts the output threshold without changing the decision policy. This is calibration without comprehension: output distributions adapt to training data while the underlying security reasoning remains absent. The weakest backbone at binary detection (DeepSeek-R1) gains the most in coarse CWE classification, revealing that detection and understanding are decoupled capabilities. The best detection score reaches only 52.1% (+2.1 pp above chance); exact CWE ranking remains below 1.3% Top-1 accuracy, confirming that current LLMs lack reliable security reasoning for systems software, regardless of fine-tuning strategy.

### [85] [Efficient and Sound Probabilistic Verification for AI Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20510v1)
*Alaia Solko-Breslin,Pramod Kaushik Mudrakarta,Mihai Christodorescu,Somesh Jha,Krishnamurthy Dj Dvijotham*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: AI agent概率验证框架，可迁移至coding agent可靠性保障

TL;DR: 提出基于分布鲁棒优化的框架，用于AI代理的运行时监控，可处理概率性策略并计算违反概率的可靠上界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有运行时监控方法仅限于确定性策略，无法处理实际应用中常见的概率性谓词或状态转换，且难以做出独立性假设以应用先前的概率推理工作。

Method: 引入分布鲁棒优化框架，计算策略违反概率的可靠上界，不依赖于谓词之间的独立性假设。

Result: 在终端和工具调用代理的标准基准测试中，该方法优于现有技术，改善了安全-效用权衡。

Conclusion: 该框架有效且高效，能够确保策略违反概率的严格界限，适用于更广泛的AI代理安全场景。

中文摘要：确保在复杂数字环境中运行的AI代理的安全性已成为关键需求，而运行时监控方法（使用Datalog等形式语言制定和执行策略）提供了一种有前景的解决方案。然而，现有方法仅限于确定性策略。在AI代理的许多实际应用中，需要在存在歧义的情况下执行安全策略，导致概率性谓词或状态转换（例如，每次调用时都有一定失败概率的解分类器或个人可识别信息检测器）。此外，在许多此类应用中，不容易做出必要的独立性假设来调用先前关于Datalog中概率推理的工作。我们通过引入一种基于分布鲁棒优化的合理且高效的框架来解决这一问题，该框架计算策略违反概率的可靠上界，而不考虑谓词之间可能存在的相关性。在终端和工具调用代理的标准基准测试中，我们展示了我们的方法优于现有技术，并改善了安全-效用权衡，同时确保策略违反概率的严格界限。

Original abstract: Securing AI agents that operate in complex digital environments has become a critical need, and runtime monitoring approaches that formulate and enforce policies expressed in a formal language like Datalog offer a promising solution. However, existing approaches are restricted to deterministic policies. In many practical applications of AI agents, there is a need to enforce security policies in the face of ambiguity, leading to probabilistic predicates or state transitions (for example, a declassifier or Personally Identifiable Information (PII) detector that has some failure probability on each invocation). Furthermore, in many such applications, one cannot easily make the independence assumptions necessary to invoke prior work on probabilistic inference in Datalog. We address this by introducing a sound and efficient framework for such verification based on distributionally robust optimization, computing sound upper bounds on the probability of policy violation regardless of possible correlations between predicates. On standard benchmarks for terminal and tool calling agents, we demonstrate that our approach outperforms prior art and improves the security-utility trade-off while ensuring rigorous bounds on the probability of policy violation.

### [86] [Sovereign Execution Broker: Enforcing Certificate-Bound Authority in Agentic Control Planes](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20520v2)
*Jun He,Deying Yu*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: agent执行安全边界，可迁移至coding agent安全架构

TL;DR: 提出主权执行代理（SEB），在运行时强制证书绑定的权限，确保自主代理的变更操作得到认证和审计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有访问控制和保证层无法在变更时刻提供强制性的认证权限执行点，生产环境中的变更权限不应存在于非确定性推理过程中。

Method: SEB 使用由主权保证边界（SAB）颁发的证书，验证变更与执行合约的一致性，检查有效期、策略和撤销状态，生成限域身份，调用基础设施 API 并记录签名记录，通过分离提议、准入和执行实现运行时强制。

Result: 在 AWS 和 Kubernetes 上评估原型，显示出可接受的延迟开销、有效的撤销传播、漂移检测能力和故障注入下的安全性。

Conclusion: SEB 将认证权限转化为短期的、可撤销的、可审计的运行时能力，为代理基础设施提供安全的变更执行边界。

中文摘要：自主代理越来越多地连接到云端、部署和数据控制工作流，但生产环境中的变更权限不应存在于非确定性推理过程中。现有的访问控制机制对身份进行授权，而保证层则认证提议的操作；两者单独都无法在变更时刻提供对认证权限的强制执行点。本文介绍了主权执行代理（SEB），一种用于证书绑定的代理基础设施的运行时强制边界。SEB 消费由主权保证边界（SAB）颁发的证书，验证请求的变更与认证的执行合约一致，检查有效期窗口、策略纪元、撤销纪元和实时状态漂移，生成限域执行身份，调用基础设施 API，并记录签名的决策和结果记录。通过分离提议、准入和执行，SEB 将认证权限转化为短期的、可撤销的、可审计的运行时能力，前提是生产变更 API 拒绝非代理身份。我们介绍了 SEB 的执行模型、证书和重放验证谓词、限域身份语义、防旁路部署模式、故障行为以及具体的原型实现。我们在 AWS 和 Kubernetes 集群上评估了原型，测量了延迟开销、撤销传播、漂移检测以及故障注入下的安全性。

Original abstract: Autonomous agents are increasingly connected to cloud, deployment, and data-control workflows, but production mutation authority should not reside inside non-deterministic reasoning processes. Existing access-control mechanisms authorize identities, while assurance layers certify proposed actions; neither alone provides a mandatory enforcement point for certified authority at the moment of mutation. This paper introduces the Sovereign Execution Broker (SEB), a runtime enforcement boundary for certificate-bound agentic infrastructure. SEB consumes certificates issued by the Sovereign Assurance Boundary (SAB), verifies that the requested mutation matches the certified execution contract, checks validity windows, policy epochs, revocation epochs, and live-state drift, mints scoped execution identity, invokes infrastructure APIs, and records signed decision and outcome records. By separating proposal, admission, and execution, SEB turns certified authority into a short-lived, revocable, auditable runtime capability, provided that production mutation APIs reject non-broker identities. We present the SEB execution model, certificate and replay-verification predicates, scoped identity semantics, bypass-prevention deployment patterns, failure behavior, and a concrete prototype implementation. We evaluate the prototype on AWS and Kubernetes clusters, measuring latency overheads, revocation propagation, drift detection, and security under fault injection.

</details>


### [87] [PromptMark: A Prompt-Guided Iterative-Feedback Framework for Source Code Watermarking](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20835v1)
*Istiaq Ahmed Fahad,Mridha Md. Nafis Fuad,Kazi Sakib*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: PromptMark是一种黑盒水印框架，通过提示引导在AI生成代码中嵌入可检测信号，保持正确性，实验效果优于基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有水印方法需要访问解码过程，不适用于黑盒商业LLM API，因此需要一种黑盒水印方法。

Method: 提出PromptMark，通过结构化输入指令（提示）引导模型生成特定命名模式，实现水印嵌入；检测使用统计测试；通过迭代反馈优化提示。

Result: 在MBPP和HumanEval上，PromptMark在保持代码正确性的同时实现了强水印可检测性，优于基线。

Conclusion: PromptMark有效解决了黑盒场景下的源代码水印问题，具有实用价值。

中文摘要：水印技术已成为确保AI生成源代码来源和可问责性的关键技术。随着大型语言模型（LLM）日益融入开发工作流程，可靠的归属仍然具有挑战性。在实践中，大多数开发者依赖于在黑盒约束下运行的商业LLM API，这使得需要访问解码过程的现有方法在实际集成中不太可行。为了解决这一限制，我们提出了PromptMark，一个黑盒、提示引导的水印框架，通过结构化输入指令将不可见但统计上可检测的信号嵌入到生成的代码中。该方法引导模型采用微妙的标识符和注释命名模式，同时保持生成代码的功能正确性和结构完整性。检测是通过统计测试进行的，这些测试设计为在不同代码长度和模型输出下保持可靠。嵌入通过迭代反馈循环进一步优化，其中提示根据水印检测分数进行更新。在MBPP和HumanEval基准上的实验表明，PromptMark在保持高代码正确性的同时，始终实现强水印可检测性，优于基线方法。

Original abstract: Watermarking has become a crucial technique for ensuring provenance and accountability in AI-generated source code. As large language models (LLMs) are increasingly integrated into development workflows, reliable attribution remains challenging. In practice, most developers rely on commercial LLM APIs operating under black-box constraints, making existing approaches that require access to the decoding process less feasible for real-world integration. To address this limitation, we propose PromptMark, a black-box, prompt-guided watermarking framework that embeds invisible yet statistically detectable signals into generated code via structured input instructions. The method steers models toward subtle identifier and comment naming patterns while preserving the functional correctness and structural integrity of the generated code. Detection is performed using statistical tests designed to remain reliable across varying code lengths and model outputs. The embedding is further refined through an iterative feedback loop, where prompts are updated based on watermark detection scores. Experiments on the MBPP and HumanEval benchmarks show that PromptMark consistently achieves strong watermark detectability while maintaining high code correctness, outperforming baseline approaches.

</details>


### [88] [Whose Agent Are You? Multi-Layer Fingerprinting and Attribution of Autonomous Web Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20910v1)
*Dayeon Kang,Hyejun Jeong,Jade Sheffey,Pubali Datta,Amir Houmansadr*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: 多层指纹识别web agent，提供agent安全评估与归因方法

TL;DR: 基于多层指纹的方法可高准确率区分AI网络代理与人类及传统爬虫。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有防御措施如robots.txt和主动机器人拦截不足以应对AI网络代理的 indiscriminate 内容抓取，需要一种有效的区分方法。

Method: 通过分析六个主流代理框架，提取网络层特征（如TLS、HTTP）和浏览器交互行为特征，构建多层指纹，并利用决策树分类器进行识别。

Result: 该框架实现了97%的准确率，成功将AI网络代理流量与人类浏览和传统爬虫区分开。

Conclusion: 跨层代理追踪是一种鲁棒且抗规避的内容保护和网络安全策略执行方案。

中文摘要：随着AI网络代理的激增，结合大型语言模型与自主浏览器级控制，网络代理的 indiscriminate 内容抓取已成为隐私和安全挑战。现有防御措施，如robots.txt和主动机器人拦截，因被广泛违反且易于规避而不足。在这项工作中，我们证明基于网络层特征（如TLS、HTTP）和浏览器交互行为的多层指纹可以有效区分AI网络代理与人类和传统爬虫。我们将此机制实现为一个程序化日志框架，可部署在实时、有仪器的域上。通过分析六个主流代理框架（AutoGen, Browser Use, Claude, Gemini, Operator, 和 Skyvern），我们揭示了这些系统在组装HTTP请求、建立TLS/HTTP连接和执行自主浏览器操作方面的潜在结构差异。将这些多层特征输入决策树分类器，我们的框架实现了高保真识别（97%准确率），成功隔离了不同的代理架构，并将代理流量与人类浏览基线和传统爬虫区分开来。我们的发现表明，跨层代理追踪为内容保护和网络安全策略执行提供了鲁棒且抗规避的策略。

Original abstract: As AI web agents proliferate, combining large language models with autonomous, browser-level control, indiscriminate content scraping by web agents has emerged as a privacy and security challenge. Existing defenses, such as robots.txt and active bot-blocking, are insufficient, as they are widely violated and easily circumvented. In this work, we demonstrate that AI web agents can be effectively distinguished from humans and traditional crawlers using a multi-layer fingerprint based on both network layer characteristics (e.g., TLS, HTTP) and browser interaction behavior. We implement this mechanism as a programmatic logging framework that can be deployed on a live, instrumented domain.
  By analyzing six prominent agent frameworks (AutoGen, Browser Use, Claude, Gemini, Operator, and Skyvern), we uncover latent structural differences in how these systems assemble HTTP requests, establish TLS/HTTP connections, and execute autonomous browser actions. Feeding these multi-layer features into a decision tree classifier, our framework achieves high-fidelity identification (97% accuracy), successfully isolating distinct agent architectures and differentiating agent traffic from both human browsing baselines and legacy crawlers. Our findings demonstrate that cross-layer agent tracking provides a robust, evasion-resistant strategy for content protection and web security policy enforcement.

中文摘要：学术论文搜索是科学研究中的核心步骤，基于LLM的搜索代理正在成为迭代式、意图驱动的文献探索的一种有前景的范式。然而，现有的基准测试不足以在真实开放文献环境下系统评估智能体学术搜索。我们提出了ScholarQuest，一个大规模的、基于分类法指导的智能体学术论文搜索基准测试。ScholarQuest基于超过1,000个计算机科学主题和四种代表性研究意图构建，包括方法导向、场景锚定、基于比较和范围限制的查询。它进一步提供了可扩展的答案构建和共享检索后端ScholarBase，以实现可重复评估。基准测试结果表明，智能体方法优于单次检索基线，但表现最佳的智能体仅达到0.314的Recall@100和0.355的Recall@All，表明仍有很大的改进空间。此外，对搜索效率、意图级别鲁棒性和失败案例的分析进一步突出了该基准测试为学术论文搜索智能体提供多维度评估信号的能力。

Original abstract: Academic paper search is a core step in scientific research, and LLM-based search agents are emerging as a promising paradigm for iterative, intent-driven literature exploration. However, existing benchmarks are insufficient for systematically evaluating agentic academic search under realistic open literature environments. We propose ScholarQuest, a large-scale, taxonomy-guided benchmark for agentic academic paper search. ScholarQuest is constructed from over 1,000 computer science topics and four representative research intents, including method-oriented, setting-anchored, comparison-based, and scope-controlled queries. It further provides scalable answer construction and a shared retrieval backend ScholarBase for reproducible evaluation. Benchmarking results show that agentic methods outperform single-shot retrieval baselines, yet the best-performing agent only achieves 0.314 Recall@100 and 0.355 Recall@All, indicating substantial room for improvement. In addition, analyses of search efficiency, intent-level robustness, and failure cases further highlight the benchmark's ability to provide multi-dimensional evaluation signals for academic paper search agents.

Original abstract: We propose a model-grounded RAG-based AI economist with an agentic framework for economic scenario analysis using large language models (LLMs) and knowledge graphs. Based on this motivation, this study proposes an RAG-based AI economist, which utilizes knowledge graphs including economic data and theory and LLM-based agents to plan the analysis, retrieve relevant evidence, select appropriate models, and generate reports. In our framework, we do not produce quantitative claims directly with the language model alone; instead, we generate narratives grounded in explicit model-based computations and linked to the retrieved evidence via AI agents. We refer to our framework as an AI economist agent. We evaluate the AI economist agent in two applications: economist report generation for U.S. inflation persistence and Federal Reserve policy, and bank stress-test narrative generation for U.S. commercial real estate refinancing stress. ### [91] [AURA: Adaptive Uncertainty-aware Refinement for LLM-as-a-Judge Auditing](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19714v1)
*Zilong Zhang,Yi-Ting Hung,Weiyi He,Junxi Zhang,Lei Ding,Chi-Kuang Yeh*

Main category: stat.ML

Selection reason: LLM-as-judge审计框架，涉及agent评估不确定性。

TL;DR: AURA是一个自适应不确定性感知的细化框架，用于在有限人工验证下审计LLM作为评判者的成对决策。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 人工评估成本高且难以扩展，LLM评判者存在偏见；现有审计方法依赖于事先干净的监督信号，但该假设在LLM评估中很脆弱。

Method: AURA迭代学习人类一致性信号，传播可靠证据，并优先将不确定比较提交人工审查；将评判者信任视为随证据积累逐步细化的潜在量。

Result: 在合成和真实成对LLM答案数据上的全面评估表明AURA有效。

Conclusion: AURA提供了一个稳定的细化过程，在有限人工验证下有效审计LLM评判者。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLMs）越来越多地被用作开放式生成的评判者，因为大规模人工评估通常昂贵且难以扩展，但它们的偏好仍然是不完美的人类判断代理。现有的审计管道通常假设事先存在可靠的示例子集或干净的监督信号，例如来自人工注释、启发式过滤或强评判者的输出。在LLM评估中，这个假设是脆弱的：初始分割可能继承评判者偏差，而人工验证通常过于稀缺，无法在大规模上定义稳定的群体。我们提出了AURA，一个自适应不确定性感知的细化框架，用于在选定的人工验证下审计成对LLM作为评判者的决策。AURA迭代地学习人类一致性信号，传播可靠证据，并优先将不确定的比较提交给人工审查。关键思想是将对评判者的信任视为一个潜在量，随着证据的积累而逐步细化。我们提供了一个紧凑的公式、一个稳定的细化过程，以及在合成和真实成对LLM答案数据上的全面评估。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly used as judges for open-ended generation, as large-scale human evaluation is often expensive and difficult to scale, yet their preferences remain imperfect proxies for human judgment. Existing auditing pipelines often assume that a reliable subset of examples or clean supervision signals are available beforehand, for example from human annotation, heuristic filtering, or the outputs of strong judges. In LLM evaluation, this assumption is fragile: the initial split may inherit judge bias, while human verification is typically too scarce to define stable groups at scale. We propose AURA, an adaptive uncertainty--aware refinement framework for auditing pairwise LLM--as--a--judge decisions under selected human verification. AURA iteratively learns a human-consistency signal, propagates reliable evidence, and prioritizes uncertain comparisons for human review. The key idea is to treat trust in a judge as a latent quantity that is progressively refined as evidence accumulates. We provide a compact formulation, a stable refinement procedure, and a comprehensive evaluation on both synthetic and real pairwise LLM-answer data.

</details>
